Transmission [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the transmission of Master Information Block (MIB) data on the Broadcast Control Channel (BCCH) in a 5G network. The diagram depicts interactions between four entities: UE (User Equipment), 5G-L1-DL (5G Layer 1 Downlink), 5G-L2-PS (5G Layer 2 Packet Switched), and 5G-CP (5G Control Plane). The sequence of events is as follows: 1. PsCell_SystemInfoConfigurationReq (MIB) : The 5G-L2-PS entity sends a request to the 5G-CP entity, containing the Master Information Block (MIB) configuration. 2. MIB content stored : The 5G-CP entity acknowledges and stores the MIB content. 3. PsCell_SystemInfoConfigurationResp : The 5G-CP entity sends a response back to the 5G-L2-PS entity, confirming the configuration. 4. PBCH scheduling : The 5G-L2-PS entity initiates the scheduling of the Physical Broadcast Channel (PBCH). 5. DIData_SsBlockSendReq (every SS burst slot) : The 5G-L2-PS entity sends a request to the 5G-L1-DL entity to send data for the SS block, which occurs every Synchronization Signal (SS) burst slot. 6. Loop : A loop is indicated, suggesting that the subsequent actions are repeated. 7. PBCH (MIB), PSS, SSS : Within the loop, the 5G-L1-DL entity transmits the PBCH containing the MIB, along with Primary Synchronization Signal (PSS) and Secondary Synchronization Signal (SSS), to the UE. The title of the diagram is "DL Data on BCCH: Master Information Block Transmission".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_2333.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to file "5G_L1L2_FLOW_240 DL Data on BCCH - Master Information Block Transmission.signalling" : (ID: 11194142)

on BCCH: System Information Block type 1 Transmission 11194160: DL Data on BCCH: System Information Block type 1 Transmission [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating "DL Data on BCCH: System Information Block type 1 Transmission". The diagram depicts interactions between four entities: UE, 5G-L1-DL, 5G-L2-PS, and 5G-CP, with a Timer indicated by a dashed line. The sequence of events is as follows: 1. 5G-L2-PS sends a PsCell_SystemInfoConfigurationReq (SIB1) to 5G-CP . 2. 5G-CP responds with PsCell_SystemInfoConfigurationResp . This interaction is associated with an "SI Window or Modification Period". 3. 5G-L2-PS receives "SIB1 content stored (inactive context)". 4. 5G-L2-PS initiates "SIB1 context activation". This is synchronized with an "SI window period". 5. 5G-L2-PS performs "Active SIB1 context scheduling". This is synchronized with an "SI transmission period". 6. Within a loop, 5G-L2-PS engages in "SIB1 transmission or retransmission". This is associated with "$FN and slot for SI (SS/PBCH)". 7. Within another loop, 5G-L2-PS sends "SIB1 per SS/PBCH". 8. Following this, 5G-L2-PS sends three requests to 5G-L1-DL : * DIData_PdcchSendReq * DIData_PdschSendReq * DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq 9. Finally, 5G-L1-DL transmits PDCCH (DCI) and PDSCH (SIB1) . The diagram uses vertical lines to represent the lifelines of each entity and horizontal arrows to indicate messages exchanged between them. Dashed arrows represent asynchronous messages or signals. The "Loop" indicators suggest repeated actions. The diagram is organized into distinct phases of SIB1 transmission.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_2335.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to file "5G_L1L2_FLOW_242 DL Data on BCCH - SIB1 Transmission.signalling" : (ID: 11194160)

Transmission [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the transmission of System Information (SI) messages over the Broadcast Control Channel (BCCH) in a 5G network. The diagram depicts interactions between three entities: UE (User Equipment), 5G-L1-DL (5G Layer 1 Downlink), 5G-L2-PS (5G Layer 2 Packet Switched), and 5G-CP (5G Control Plane). A Timer is also shown as a dashed line. The diagram shows the following sequence of events: 1. PsCell_SystemInfoConfigurationReq (SI-Msg) : The 5G-L2-PS entity sends a request to the 5G-CP entity to configure system information messages. 2. SI-Msg content stored (inactive context) : The 5G-CP entity stores the SI message content in an inactive context. 3. PsCell_SystemInfoConfigurationResp : The 5G-CP entity responds to the 5G-L2-PS entity. 4. SI Window or Modification Period : A period related to SI window or modification is indicated. 5. SI-Msg context activation : The 5G-L2-PS entity activates the SI message context. 6. SI window period : A specific SI window period is shown. 7. Active SI-Msg context scheduling : The 5G-L2-PS entity schedules the active SI message context. 8. SI transmission period : A period for SI transmission is indicated. 9. SI-Msg transmission or retransmission : The 5G-L2-PS entity transmits or retransmits SI messages. This is shown within a loop. 10. SFN and slot for SI (SS/PBCH) : The SFN (System Frame Number) and slot for SI (SS/PBCH) are determined. 11. SI-Msg per SS/PBCH : SI messages are prepared per SS/PBCH. This is also within a loop. 12. DIData_PdcchSendReq : The 5G-L2-PS entity sends a request to the 5G-L1-DL to send data on PDCCH (Physical Downlink Control Channel). 13. DIData_PdschSendReq : The 5G-L2-PS entity sends a request to the 5G-L1-DL to send data on PDSCH (Physical Downlink Shared Channel). 14. DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq : The 5G-L2-PS entity sends a request to the 5G-L1-DL to send the PDSCH payload transmission block. 15. PDCCH (DCI) : The 5G-L1-DL entity transmits a PDCCH with DCI (Downlink Control Information) to the UE. 16. PDSCH (SI-Msg) : The 5G-L1-DL entity transmits the PDSCH containing the SI message to the UE. The diagram uses loops to indicate repetitive actions in the transmission process. The dashed lines represent control signals or timing indications.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_2337.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to file "5G_L1L2_FLOW_244 DL Data on BCCH - SI Message Transmission.signalling" : (ID: 11194176)

[CB015504-C]
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of "DL Data on DCCH in gNB-DU". The diagram depicts interactions between several entities: UE, 5G-L1-UL, 5G-L1-DL, 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-LO, 5G-L2-HI (DU), and 5G-CP-RT. A timer is also shown on the right side.
The diagram outlines a series of messages and actions exchanged between these entities. Key messages include:
\* **(1) DL RRC message transfer over F1-C interface:** This message is not visible to U-Plane.
\* **(2) HiSgnlDu\_SrbSendReq:** Sent from 5G-L2-HI (DU) to 5G-CP-RT.
\* **(3) LoData\_DIRicPduSendReq** and **(3) LoData\_DISrbRlcPduSendReq:** These messages are related to data PDU for SRB and are exchanged between 5G-L2-LO and 5G-L2-HI (DU).
\* **(3.1) SrbScheduleTimer start:** Initiated by 5G-CP-RT.
\* **(4) LoCtrl\_DIBufferStatusInd:** Sent from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-L2-LO.
\* **(5) Prepare and schedule TB:** An action performed by 5G-L2-LO.
\* **(6) UC: DL HARQ Tx:** An action performed by 5G-L1-DL.
\* **(7) LoData\_SrbDataDeliveryStatusInd:** Sent from 5G-L2-LO to 5G-L2-HI (DU), indicating successful transfer of RLC SN to MAC.
\* **(7.1) SrbScheduleTimer stop:** An action performed by 5G-CP-RT.
\* **(8) respFlag == TRUE:** A conditional check within an optional block.
\* **(9) HiSgnlDu\_SrbSendResp:** Sent from 5G-L2-HI (DU) to 5G-CP-RT.
\* **(10) rlcResetRequired == TRUE:** Another conditional check within an optional block, leading to RLC re-establishment.
\* **(11) SrbScheduleTimer expiry:** Triggered by the timer.
\* **(12) HiUserDu\_BearerErrorInd:** Sent from 5G-L2-HI (DU) to 5G-CP-RT, indicating a bearer error.
\* **(13) RLC PDU max ReTx reached:** A conditional check within an optional block.
\* **(14) HiUserDu\_BearerErrorInd:** Another bearer error indication.
\* **(15) UC: UL Data on DCCH in gNB-DU (RLC acknowledgement):** An action performed by UE.
The diagram also includes notes such as "Before CB015504-C", "CB015504-C", "Data PDU for SRB", ">>Successful transfer of RLC SN<<", "RlcSnSubmittedToMac indicates: the successful transfer of RLC PDU to MAC", ">>SrbScheduleTimer timeout<<", and "bearerError Cause=SrbSendReq Timeout. CP-RT would just log this message."[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/12807221\_DL Data on DCCH in gNB-DU.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

DL Data on DTCH (RLC AM)
[CB015504-C]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the flow of DL (Downlink) data on DTCH (Data Transmission Channel) using RLC AM (Radio Link Control Acknowledged Mode). The diagram depicts interactions between several network entities: UE (User Equipment), 5G-L1-UL (5G Layer 1 Uplink), 5G-L1-DL (5G Layer 1 Downlink), 5G-L2-PS (5G Layer 2 Packet Switching), 5G-L2-LO (5G Layer 2 Lower Layer), 5G-L2-HI (DU) (5G Layer 2 Higher Layer - Data Unit), 5G-L2-HI (CU) (5G Layer 2 Higher Layer - Control Unit), 5G-CP-NRT (5G Control Plane - Non-Real Time), and SGW (Serving Gateway).
The diagram shows a sequence of messages exchanged between these entities, numbered from (1) to (11).
Here's a breakdown of the messages and interactions:
\* **(1) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd:** Sent from 5G-L2-LO to 5G-L2-HI (DU), indicating the delivery status of UE data. This message is associated with "DL data path status indication (Flow Control)".
\* **(2) GTP-U PDU:** Sent from 5G-L2-HI (DU) to 5G-L2-HI (CU). This message is related to "F1-U DDDS".
\* **(3) GTP-U PDU:** Sent from 5G-L2-HI (CU) to 5G-CP-NRT. This message is associated with "PDCP SDU".
\* **(4) HiUserCu\_PdcpMaxCountInd:** An optional message sent from 5G-L2-HI (CU) to SGW. It indicates a "PDCP COUNT rollover indication".
\* **(5) GTP-U PDU:** Sent from 5G-L2-HI (CU) to 5G-L2-LO. This message is associated with "F1-U DL USER DATA".
\* **(6) LoData\_DIRIcPduSendReq:** A message sent from 5G-L2-LO to itself (indicated by the arrow pointing back to the same lifeline). This message is labeled "Before CB015504-C" and is a "Data PDU".
\* **(6) LoData\_DIDrbRlcPduSendReq:** Another message sent from 5G-L2-LO to itself, labeled "CB015504-C". This is also a "Data PDU".
\* **(7) LoData\_DIRIcStatusPduSendReq:** Sent from 5G-L2-LO to 5G-L2-HI (DU). This is a "Control PDU".
\* **(8) LoCtrl\_DIBufferStatusInd:** Sent from 5G-L2-HI (DU) to 5G-L2-PS.
\* **(9) UC: DL HARQ Tx:** A message originating from the UE, indicating Downlink HARQ Transmission. This is marked with a "ref" tag.
\* **(10) UC: UL Data on UL-SCH (RLC acknowledgement):** A message originating from the UE, indicating Uplink Data on UL-SCH with RLC acknowledgement. This is also marked with a "ref" tag.
\* **(11) HiUserDu\_BearerErrorInd:** An optional message sent from 5G-L2-HI (DU) to 5G-L2-PS. This message indicates that "5G-L2-HI (DU) indicates to C-Plane unsuccessful delivery of RLC PDU (maxReTx threshold)".
The diagram visually represents the complex communication flow for downlink data transmission in a 5G network, highlighting the roles of different layers and units in handling data, control, and status indications.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/12815468\_DL Data on DTCH (RLC AM).png[/image\_path][/image-0]

### 8.2.1.8 DL HARQ Tx

#### 8.2.1.8.0-1 DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx 11194532: DL HARQ Tx [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the Downlink (DL) Hybrid Automatic Repeat Request (HARQ) Transmission (Tx) process in a 5G system. The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities: UE (User Equipment), 5G-L1-UL (5G Layer 1 Uplink), 5G-L1-DL (5G Layer 1 Downlink), 5G-L2-PS (5G Layer 2 Packet Switched), and 5G-L2-LO (5G Layer 2 Lower Layer). The diagram is divided into two main sections: the initial transmission and retransmissions. Initial Transmission: * 5G-L2-PS initiates the process by performing DL MAC Scheduling . * It sends request messages to 5G-L1-DL and 5G-L1-UL on a carrier allocation basis. * 5G-L2-LO assembles the Transport Block (TB) sequentially for each 5G-L1-DL system component and transmits it on the carrier allocation basis. * 5G-L2-LO sends a DIData_PdcchSendReq (DCI) to 5G-L1-DL . * 5G-L1-DL sends a DIData_PdschSendReq to 5G-L2-PS . * 5G-L2-PS sends a LoCtrl_PduMuxReq to 5G-L2-LO . * 5G-L2-LO sends a DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq (DL HARQ Tx) to 5G-L1-DL . * 5G-L1-DL sends PDCCH and PDSCH (TB) to the UE . * The UE receives the data and sends back UIData_PucchReceiveReq to 5G-L1-DL . * 5G-L1-DL then sends UIData_PucchReceiveRespPs and UIData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD to 5G-L2-PS . * The DL HARQ feedback of all configured Component Carriers (CCs) in the UE (Joint-UCI) is received via the 5G-L1 of the UE's PSCell. Retransmission (Loop): The diagram indicates an optional loop that continues "until HARQ ACK is received OR numOfTx reaches maxDIHarqTx". * DL HARQ ReTx in case of HARQ N : This section details the retransmission process. * 5G-L2-PS performs DL MAC Scheduling again. * It sends DIData_PdcchSendReq (DCI) to 5G-L1-DL . * 5G-L1-DL sends DIData_PdschSendReq to 5G-L2-PS . * 5G-L2-PS sends LoCtrl_PduMuxReq to 5G-L2-LO . * 5G-L2-LO sends DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq (DL HARQ ReTx) to 5G-L1-DL . * 5G-L1-DL sends PDCCH and PDSCH (TB ReTx) to the UE . * The UE receives the retransmitted data and sends back UIData_PucchReceiveReq to 5G-L1-DL . * 5G-L1-DL then sends UIData_PucchReceiveRespPs and UIData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD to 5G-L2-PS . A note indicates that HARQ retransmission is done via the same 5G-L1 where the original transmission was done.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_2385.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to the "5G_L1L2_FLOW_260_DL HARQ Tx.signalling" file: (ID: 11194532)

MSC for illustration:
 
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a process related to segmented RLC data PDUs, likely within a telecommunications context. It includes textual explanations and a flowchart-like representation of actions and states.
**Textual Explanation:**
The text at the top provides context for the diagram, explaining actions performed by L2-LO and L2-PS entities per slot. Key points include:
\* **L2-LO:** Sends `LoCtrl_DIBufferStatusInd` at every slot start if new DL data is received or an initial transmission occurs.
\* **L2-PS:**
\* Initiates DL scheduling at the start of a DL slot.
\* Avoids allocations smaller than `rrmMinDIAllocationSize` (26 bytes).
\* Allocates extra `rrmMaxMacPlusRlcHeaderSize` (8 bytes) if the DL buffer can be emptied, to compensate for MAC/RLC header inaccuracies from the previous slot.
\* Saves the amount of scheduled bytes in `rrmScheduledDIData_bytes`.
\* Subtracts scheduled bytes from `bufferedBytes`, noting that the result might not reflect added MAC/RLC headers, leading to a buffer level that is "too small" (indicated by green parts in the diagram).
\* Evaluates `LoCtrl_DIBufferStatusInd` and copies the received DL buffer level to `bufferedBytes`. This might not reflect bytes scheduled in the same slot, leading to a buffer level that is "too high" (indicated by red parts).
\* After evaluating `LoCtrl_DIBufferStatusInd`, it subtracts `rrmScheduledDIData_bytes` from `bufferedBytes`, improving buffer level accuracy (indicated by dark blue parts).
**Improvements achieved with the Pronto correction:**
\* Improved buffer level accuracy in L2-PS.
\* No scheduling of useless DL transmissions (only MAC PDUs with padding).
\* Fewer DL transmissions needed to empty the DL buffer.
**Diagrammatic Representation:**
The diagram depicts a sequence of events and states, using boxes for actions/states and arrows for transitions.
**Section 1: Initial State**
\* A box labeled "buffer level = 100 bytes" is shown, with a wavy arrow pointing downwards.
\* This leads to a box labeled "bufferedBytes = 100".
**Section 2: First Scheduling Event**
\* From "bufferedBytes = 100", a transition occurs to a series of actions:
\* "Reset rrmScheduledDIData\_bytes = 0."
\* "Available: 60 bytes."
\* "Schedule max{ 60 bytes, rrmMinDIAllocationSize bytes } = 60 bytes."
\* "Set rrmScheduledDIData\_bytes = 60."
\* "Set bufferedBytes = 40."
\* This sequence is followed by a box labeled "LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq(60 bytes )".
**Section 3: Second Scheduling Event**
\* A box labeled "buffer level = 47 bytes" is shown, with a wavy arrow pointing downwards.
\* This leads to a box labeled "LoCtrl\_DIBufferStatusind(bufferedBytes = 47)".
\* From this, a transition occurs to:
\* "DIBufferStatusind in event queue."
\* "Reset rrmScheduledDIData\_bytes = 0."
\* "Available: >= 40 bytes + rrmMaxMacPlusRlcHeaderSize bytes."
\* "Schedule max{ 40 bytes + rrmMaxMacPlusRlcHeaderSize bytes, rrmMinDIAllocationSize bytes } = 48 bytes."
\* "Set rrmScheduledDIData\_bytes = 48."
\* This is followed by a box labeled "LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq(48 bytes )".
**Section 4: Final State**
\* From "LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq(48 bytes )", a transition occurs to:
\* "Set bufferedBytes = 0."
\* "Send MAC PDU with payload and padding."
\* "buffer level = 0 bytes"
\* This leads to "LoCtrl\_DIBufferStatusind(bufferedBytes = 0)".
\* The final sequence of actions is:
\* "Read DIBufferStatusind from queue."
\* "Set bufferedBytes = 47."
\* "Set bufferedBytes = max(0, bufferedBytes - rrmScheduledDIData\_bytes} = 0."[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2388.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
 
 
The example of > 6GHz:
 
 
 
The DL buffer level handling in 5G-L2-PS (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4559\_replaced([11186978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is illustrated with MSCs for some examples. The examples show the usage of the parameters bufferedBytes and rrmScheduledDlData\_bytes[.] for below 6GHz (scs = 15 or 30) and above 6 GHz (scs = 120).
 
\* bufferedBytes: See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4561\_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
\* rrmScheduledDlData\_bytes: See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4561\_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 8.2.1.10.2 DL Data Forwarding during Inter-gNB HO

##### 8.2.1.10.2.1 Call flow:

###### 8.2.1.10.2.1.0-2 Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: 13359434: Call flow: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of DL data forwarding for ENDC Inter gNB mobility. The diagram depicts interactions between two entities, "5G-L2-HI (CU) Target-gNB" and "5G-L2-HI (CU) Source-gNB", along with auxiliary entities like "SGW", "MeNB", and "Timer". The diagram is divided into two main scenarios: "Direct DL data forwarding over X2-U DL data forwarding tunnel" and "Indirect DL data forwarding over X2-U DL data forwarding tunnel". Scenario 1: Direct DL data forwarding over X2-U DL data forwarding tunnel This scenario is further broken down into two alternative paths based on the reception of an "End Marker" or the expiry of a timer. * Path 1: Upon DL End Marker reception * The process starts with "DL Data Forwarding" from Source-gNB to Target-gNB over the X2 DRB Forwarding Tunnel. * This is followed by a "GTP-U PDU (DL End Marker)" sent from Source-gNB to Target-gNB. * A yellow box indicates that once DL data forwarding is completed, the End Marker is sent as the last GTP-U packet over the DL data forwarding X2-U tunnel. Any user data received from SGW after the End Marker is discarded. * Subsequently, "DL End Marker" is received by Target-gNB from Source-gNB over the X2 DRB Forwarding Tunnel. * A "stop endMarkerTimer" message is sent. * Path 2: End of DL data forwarding upon endMarkerTimer expiry * This path is triggered by an "endMarkerTimer expiry" message. Scenario 2: Indirect DL data forwarding over X2-U DL data forwarding tunnel This scenario also has two alternative paths based on the reception of an "End Marker" or the expiry of a timer. * Path 1: Upon DL End Marker reception * The process begins with "DL data forwarding" from Source-gNB to Target-gNB over the X2-U DRB Forwarding Tunnel. * Then, "DL data forwarding" from Source-gNB to Target-gNB over the X2-UDRB Forwarding Tunnel. * A "GTP-U PDU (DL End Marker)" is sent from Source-gNB to Target-gNB. * Another "GTP-U PDU (DL End Marker)" is sent from Source-gNB to Target-gNB over the X2-U DRB Forwarding Tunnel. * Similar to the direct scenario, a yellow box explains that once DL data forwarding is completed, the End Marker is sent as the last GTP-U packet over the DL data forwarding X2-U tunnel. Any user data received from SGW after the End Marker is discarded. * "GTP-U PDU (DL End Marker)" is received by Target-gNB from Source-gNB over the X2-U DRB Forwarding Tunnel. * A "stop endMarkerTimer" message is sent. * Path 2: End of DL data forwarding upon endMarkerTimer expiry * This path is triggered by an "endMarkerTimer expiry" message. At the bottom of the diagram, a general note states: "DL data forwarding is completed. Any user data received over X2-U DL data forwarding tunnel after receiving End marker message or after End marker timer expiry shall be discarded." The diagram also includes a legend at the top and bottom with the labels "5G-L2-HI (CU)", "Target-gNB", "Source-gNB", "SGW", "MeNB", and "Timer". ### 8.2.1.12 DL Data Forwarding (SA)

#### 8.2.1.12.1 DL Data Forwarding for Inter-gNB mobility

##### 8.2.1.12.1.1 Call flow:

###### 8.2.1.12.1.1.0-2 Call flow: 13431177: Call flow: 13431177: Call flow: 13431177: Call flow: 13431177: Call flow: 13431177: Call flow: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating "DL Data Forwarding for SA Inter gNB Mobility". The diagram depicts interactions between a Target-gNB and a Source-gNB, both utilizing 5G-L2-HI (CU) interfaces. It also shows interactions with UPF (User Plane Function) and a Timer. The diagram is divided into two main sections, indicated by alt blocks, representing different scenarios of data forwarding. Section 1: Direct DL DRB data forwarding over Xn-U forwarding tunnel This section details the direct forwarding of Downlink (DL) DRB (Data Radio Bearer) data over an Xn-U forwarding tunnel. * Step 1: The process begins with a directive for direct DL DRB data forwarding over the Xn-U forwarding tunnel. * Step 2: DL Data Forwarding occurs on the Xn-U DRB Forwarding Tunnel. * Step 3: A GTP-U PDU (DL End Marker) is sent. * A note indicates that in case of direct data forwarding, only DL DRB data forwarding is used. * Another note explains that once DL data forwarding is completed, an End Marker is sent as the last GTP-U packet over the DL data forwarding Xn-U tunnel. Any user data received from UPF after the End Marker is discarded. This section further breaks down into two sub-sections using alt blocks: * [(4) End of DL data forwarding upon DL End Marker reception]: * Step 5: DL End Marker is received on the Xn DRB Forwarding Tunnel. * Step 6: The endMarkerTimer is stopped. * [(7) End of DL data forwarding upon endMarkerTimer expiry]: * Step 8: The endMarkerTimer expires. * [[CB012328-D] (9) Concurrent Handover or Bearer Type Change Procedure]: * Step 10: Concurrent Handover or Bearer Type Change Procedure (13431127) is initiated. Section 2: Indirect DL DRB/PDU session data forwarding over Ng-U forwarding tunnel This section describes the indirect forwarding of DL DRB/PDU session data over an Ng-U forwarding tunnel. * A note states that in case of indirect data forwarding, data can be forwarded from one gNB to another via a PDU session or DRB forwarding tunnel over Ng-U. * Step 12: DL data forwarding occurs on the Ng-U Forwarding Tunnel. * Step 13: DL data forwarding occurs on the Ng-U Forwarding Tunnel. * Step 14 &amp; 15: GTP-U PDU (DL End Marker) is sent on the Ng-U Forwarding Tunnel. * A note explains that once DL data forwarding is completed, an End Marker is sent as the last GTP-U packet over the DL DRB/PDU Session forwarding tunnel. Any user data received from UPF after the End Marker is discarded. This section also breaks down into two sub-sections using alt blocks: * [(16) End of DL data forwarding upon DL End Marker reception]: * Step 17: GTP-U PDU (DL End Marker) is received on the Ng-U Forwarding Tunnel. * Step 18: The endMarkerTimer is stopped. * [(19) End of DL data forwarding upon endMarkerTimer expiry]: * Step 20: The endMarkerTimer expires. * [[CB012328-D] (21) Concurrent Handover or Bearer Type Change Procedure]: * Step 22: Concurrent Handover or Bearer Type Change Procedure (13431127) is initiated. Finally, a concluding note states that DL data forwarding is completed. Any user data received from the DL DRB/PDU Session forwarding tunnel after receiving the End marker message or after the End marker timer expiry shall be discarded.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/8899e2d9-e318-4a5f-9fc2-666ee00f7f35.png[/image_path][/image-0] [CB012328-SR-D] Conv erted to PlantUML [CB012328-SR-D] **** (ID: 13431177)

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating data transfer over the F1-U/Xn-U interface in a 5G network, specifically focusing on Downlink (DL) data on the DTCH (Dedicated Control Transport Channel) using RLC AM (Acknowledged Mode).
The diagram depicts interactions between several network functions:
- **gNB-MN (gNB-Mobile Network)**: Represented by the "5G-L2-LO" lifeline on the left.
- **gNB-SN (gNB-Serving Node)**: Represented by "5G-L2-HI (DU)", "5G-L2-LO", "5G-L2-HI (CU)" lifelines in the middle.
- **UPF (User Plane Function)**: Represented by the "UPF" lifeline on the far right.
The diagram shows messages exchanged between these entities, categorized by interfaces:
- **F1-U interface**: Between gNB-MN and gNB-SN.
- **Xn-U interface**: Between different gNB-SN instances or between gNB-SN and other gNBs.
Key messages and interactions include:
- **Initial data flow**: Message (1) "F1-U interface" indicates the start of data flow.
- **UE Data Delivery Status**: Messages (2) and (10) "LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusind" are sent from gNB-MN to gNB-SN, indicating the status of data delivery to the User Equipment (UE).
- **GTP-U PDUs**: Various GTP-U (GPRS Tunneling Protocol - User Plane) packets are exchanged, carrying data and control information. These include:
- (3) "GTP-U PDU F1-U DDDS"
- (4) "GTP-U PDU PDCP SDU"
- (5) "GTP-U PDU PDCP PDU"
- (11) "GTP-U PDU Xn-U DDDS"
- (12) "GTP-U PDU PDCP SDU"
- (13) "GTP-U PDU PDCP SDU"
- **RLC PDU Type**: Messages (6) and (14) indicate the type of RLC PDU being processed.
- **RLC Data and Status PDUs**: The core of the diagram shows RLC layer interactions within the gNB-SN.
- **Before CB015504-C**: This section, marked in red, shows messages related to RLC data transmission.
- (7) "LoData\_DIRIcPduSendReq DL RLC Data PDU": Request to send RLC Data PDU.
- **CB015504-C**: This section, marked in blue, shows messages related to RLC data transmission, possibly with different configurations or conditions.
- (7) "LoData\_DIDrbRIcPduSendReq DL RLC Data PDU": Request to send RLC Data PDU.
- (8) "LoData\_DIRIcStatusPduSendReq DL RLC Status PDU": Request to send RLC Status PDU.
- (15) "LoData\_DIRIcPduSendReq DL RLC Data PDU" and "LoData\_DIDrbRIcPduSendReq DL RLC Data PDU": Similar to (7), indicating RLC Data PDU requests.
- (16) "LoData\_DIRIcStatusPduSendReq DL RLC Status PDU": Similar to (8), indicating RLC Status PDU requests.
- **Xn-U Interface**: Message (9) "Xn-U interface" signifies communication over this interface.
The diagram uses "alt" blocks to represent alternative flows or conditions, and dashed boxes to group related messages or indicate specific processing stages. The overall diagram illustrates the complex interplay of different protocol layers (GTP-U, PDCP, RLC) and interfaces in delivering downlink data to the UE.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/12816308\_DL\_Data\_on\_DTCH\_RLC\_AM\_over\_F1\_Xn\_Interface.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

It also mentions that "First response message can be received before last request message has been sent". Radio link resume OR 2. DL Radio link resume OR 3. UL Radio link resume OR * This ultimately results in "PDCP DL data transmission over X2 -U interface is resumed". ## 8.2.2 DL Data Transfer (MAC level, inter L2-RT case, DL CA)

### 8.2.2.0-2 DL Data Transfer (MAC level, inter L2-RT case, DL CA) Some terminology (ID: 11195571)

**8.2.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11195584`)

DL Data Transfer (MAC level, inter L2-RT case, DL CA)
Remote L2-RT

In the inter L2-RT architecture, the remote 5G-L2-PS (or remote 5G-L2-LO) designates a 5G-L2-PS (or 5G-L2-LO) supporting a serving Cell (which might be an SCell or the P(S)Cell) that is not colocated with another serving Cell (which might be the P(S)Cell or an SCell)).

Remote SCell

In the inter L2-RT architecture, the remote SCell designates an SCell that is not collocated with the PCell in the same L2-RT instance.

[5GC001167-I]

Notes: for multiple CCs(>2CC) CA, one Pcell may have several remote Scells, one Scell may have several remote Pcell. The call flow only present relationship between any 1 Pcell and any of 1 Scell.

[End 5GC001167-I]

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "CA SCell activation (Multi L2-RT) Successful case". It depicts the interactions between different components, primarily gNB\_DU, Primary L2RT, and Secondary L2RT, along with PCell and SCell functionalities.
The diagram is structured with lifelines representing these components and messages exchanged between them over time. The primary L2RT is divided into PCell 5G-L1-UL, PCell 5G-L1-DL, PCell 5G-L2PS, PCell 5G-L2-LO, and a Timer. The Secondary L2RT includes SCell 5G-L2-PS, SCell 5G-L2-LO, and a Timer.
The sequence of events starts with the UE being inactive in the PCell and SCell being added but not activated. The process involves an activation decision, followed by a transient PUCCH phase. The diagram then shows the start of an SCell activate timer and its potential expiry.
Following this, there's a phase for PUCCH scheduling for CSI reports, including beam reports, channel acquisition, and combined CQI/PMI. The diagram also details the forwarding of CSI reports to SCell and the subsequent setting of PrimaryBeamld to a valid value.
Key messages and states include:
- `WaitUeActivationAck state`
- `WaitUeReady state`
- `WaitFirstBeam state`
- `WaitTciStateAck state`
- `WaitSCellScheduleEnableAck state`
- `ActiveScheduleEnabled state`
Several conditional messages are indicated with "OPT" and "Ref", suggesting optional steps or references to specific conditions or procedures. For instance, the activation decision can be "Blind (1390-C) or buffer based (1390-D)". The diagram also shows loops for processing multiple UEs.
The diagram concludes with the completion of SCell activation in PsPeer, indicated by the `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeScheduleResp` message and the `ActiveScheduleEnabled state`.

Beam report (BF enabled), - Chan Acq (2200 disabled or before 1390-CB), - Combined CQI/PMI (2200 enabled from 1390-C (CB008577-D)or FDD BF cell (End CB008577-D)), Start forwarding of any CSI report to SCell, (6) OPT: Beam in it, BF enabled, (6.1) Successfull Forwarding of CSI reports to SCell (use case with reception of first non DTX Beam report (CB008577-D)if TDD or non DTX CSI report with CQI/PMI when cell is FDD cell with dlMimo Mode = 80(End CB008577-D)), 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_344, PrimaryBeamld set to valid value, (6.2) PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd(list of UE, modifType=sendTciPdcchReq, macCe Payload), 5G\_L2\_IF\_685, (6.3) Successfull DL HARQ Tx MAC-CE [TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH ], 5G L1L2 FLOW 259, Alt:, (6.4) SCell 5G-L2-PS marked for release, 11182654, Exit procedure, (7) Complete SCell activation in PsPeer, (7.1) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedule Req (scheduleChange=start, list of UE), 5G\_L2\_IF\_656, LOOP, PCell has activated at least one UE, For each UE in the list, BF enabled & 2200 disabled (or before 1390-CB) (CB008577-D)for TDD (End CB008577-D)), Start scheduling emission of UE specific CSI-RS for Chan Acq., OPT: [1390-D], scellDeactivationTimergNB duration is not equal to infinite, (7.2)[Start] scellDeactivationTimergNB timer, OPT: [8311-C88311-日, (sCelllnactivityReleaseTimer is not equal to infinite and NRBTS.sCellActivation Method != blind) or ext-SCell, (7.2.1) [Stop] sCelllnactivityReleaseTimer, OPT: [8311-C], sCellInactivityReleaseTimer is not equal to infinite and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod == blind, (7.3) [Start] sCellInactivity ReleaseTimer, Ref (7.4) Start Flow Control, 5G L1L2 FLOW 506, Ue in ActiveScheduleEnabled state, (7.5) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedule Resp (list successfully activated UEs with selected beam), 5G\_L2\_IF\_658

[CB008577-D] Although FDD BF SCell has only one SSB a TCI is needed when the SCell is avtivated according to [11112694: TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE with multiple active component carriers](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA). ##### 8.2.2.1.1.0-2 SCell activation Description: (ID: 11195644)

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11195650`)

SCell activation
Activation decision

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11195665`)

SCell activation
- In Blind activation mode, SCell activation takes place after reception of the PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq indicating successful SCell addition (sCellAdditionInd set to True) [PR580933] for SA and NSA and also after RA procedure completion for NSA UE[End PR580933].

* In Buffer Based activation mode, Scell activation is periodically (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2778\_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) evaluated according to  [Before 5GC001167-I]5G\_UP\_ALG\_2716\_replaced([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[5GC001167-I]5G\_UP\_ALG\_2716\_replaced([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End 5GC001167-I] [CB007873-EA] (in case no SCell release is under preparation on PCell [CB007873-F]in SA / PSCell in NSA [End CB007873-F] side) [End CB007873-EA].

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11195671`)

SCell activation
(0) Start SCell Inactivity Release Timer

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11195678`)

SCell activation
If (NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB != infinity and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod != blind) [PR708077]or ext-SCell[End PR708077]:

The SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only.

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11195686`)

SCell activation

### (1) Start of Transient PUCCH phase

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11195692`)

SCell activation
This phase is due to uncertainty about the start of UE transmission of periodic PUCCH for CSI reports after the first activation attempt of the SCell (although CSI reports are configured at SCell addition, they are not used until the SCell is activated). Any possible multiplexing with PUSCH would prevent the ability to calculate the PUSCH TB size. Therefore, PUSCH scheduling is temporarily disabled for this UE on related slots (same principle as for RRC reconfiguration at initial setup).

The Transient phase starts right after sending the first SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC CE for SCell activation (the one-piece Sub-MSC “DL HARQ Tx” does not allow to represent it accurately).

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11195700`)

SCell activation

### (2) Transmission of MAC-CE (SCell activation)

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11195708`)

SCell activation
The “DL HARQ Tx” Sub-MSC includes acknowledgment and possible repetitions of the SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC-CE.  
Successful transmission of the Activation/Deactivation MAC-CE is assumed here (refer to error cases otherwise).

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11195715`)

SCell activation

### (3) Start SCell activate timer

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11195723`)

SCell activation
This timer is (re)started upon (re)transmission of the SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC-CE (not illustrated in the Sub-MSC “DL HARQ Tx”).

The Remote SCell instance enters in “WaitUeReady” CA state to wait for guard timer expiry (refer to RG 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2792\_replaced([11121815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) that should ensure that the SCell activation is completed on UE side and that UE is ready to transmit CSI reports for SCell channel acquisition and SCell beam management with valid content. This is especially important for CSI reports for Beam Management where content validity cannot be confirmed.

Before timer expiry, CSI reports transmitted by UE are “ignored” as PCell 5G-L2-PS does not schedule any PUCCH reception in 5G-L1-UL.

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11195730`)

SCell activation

### (4)  “SCell activate timer” expiry and end of Transient PUCCH phase

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11195737`)

SCell activation
After timer expiry, UE shall transmit periodic PUCCH for CSI reports so the Transient phase ends.

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11195744`)

SCell activation

### (5)  Start PUCCH scheduling (SCell CSI reports) and report forwarding to SCell

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `13369111`)

SCell activation
After timer expiry, UE shall transmit valid CSI reports so PCell 5G-L2-PS can start scheduling the decoding of associated PUCCH in 5G-L1-UL.

Nevertheless, if Beam forming is enabled, and 2200 feature is disabled , UE reports invalid CQI-0 as SCell cannot start transmission of UE specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition before reception of beam information from the UE. In case 2200 feature is enabled[CB008577-D] for TDD SCell or the SCell is FDD with dlMimoMode = 80[End CB008577-D], CSI-RS are transmitted per cell, so the UE can send a CSI report with valid CQI and beam information (PMI) at the same time.

PCell 5G-L2-PS forwards the SCell CSI reports received from 5G-L1-UL to the SCell 5G-L2-PS in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuschReceiveIndPs (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_451 Sub-MSC for more information).

Note: One message may contain information for several CA UE activated in same SCell. 5G-L1-UL UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs or UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs messages may contain CSI reports for P(S)Cell, other SCell(s), non-CA UE or PUCCH without CSI reports (PUCCH resource Set 1 for A/N for CA-UEs) that are not included in the PsPeerCtrl messages sent to current SCell L2-PS.

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `11195755`)

SCell activation
(6) Initial beam acquisition for SCell

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11195762`)

SCell activation

### (6.1) Get initial beam from CSI report

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-8.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13369196`)

SCell activation
If Beamforming is enabled, [CB008577-D]TDD[End CB008577-D] Scell additionally needs a first CSI report with Beam Measurement with dtxMeasurements.dtx equal to nonDTX, [CB008577-D] while FDD SCell with dlMimoMode = 80 additionally needs a first nonDTX CSI report with CQI/PMI,[End CB008577-D] for this UE to acquire the initial beam prior to any DL transmission (including UE specific CSI-RS for Channel Acquisition when 2200 feature is disabled)

PCell CA state machine enters in “WaitInitBeam” state for this purpose.

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11195781`)

SCell activation

### (6.2 and 6.3) TCI State Indication MAC-CE

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11195788`)

SCell activation
The UE may not be able to receive the "MAC-CE TCI State indication for UE-specific PDCCH" on SCell PDSCH before reception of this message that explicitly set the beam the UE shall use in this SCell (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2104\_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); there is no concern for subsequent Beam updates).

So, the SCell builds the MAC-CE and sends this payload to P(S)Cell in a PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd message with modifType equal to sendTciPdcchReq.

On reception of this indication, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS schedules the transmission of this TCI State indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC-CE according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9465\_replaced([11174010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuXqrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) priority.

The subsequent PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq message implicitely acknowledge the successul transmission of this MAC-CE.

On subsequent beam updates, the TCI State indication message is sent over SCell PDSCH.

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `13337047`)

SCell activation
(6.4) Alternative: SCell 5G-L2-PS marked for release

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-8.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13337063`)

SCell activation
If SCell release procedure is triggered on PCell’s 5G-L2-PS instance (see [11182654](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showArtifactPage&artifactURI=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fresources%2FMD_Uxkzk_vOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ&artifactInModule=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fresources%2FBI_BestWfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ&oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9&componentURI=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Frm-projects%2F_Cp08QO3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw%2Fcomponents%2F_CqjVAO3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw), reception of PsUser\_UserModifyReq message (see [10976074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showArtifactPage&artifactURI=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fresources%2FMD_mOhDAPu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ&artifactInModule=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fresources%2FBI_2VEvgvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ&oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9&componentURI=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Frm-projects%2F_Cp08QO3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw%2Fcomponents%2F_CqjVAO3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw)) with remoteScellToReleaseList IE indicating SCell(s) to be released), 5G-L2-PS shall exit the SCell activation procedure for the given SCell.

Otherwise, skip this step.

Rationale: Race condition protection between the ongoing SCell activation procedure and the new SCell release procedure on PCell side.

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-9**  (ID: `11195795`)

SCell activation

### (7) SCell activation on SCell side

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-9.0-3**  (ID: `11195814`)

SCell activation
If Beamforming is enabled, the sequence may be initiated two times per slot: on reception of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs for some UEs and on reception of UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs for other UEs.

(7.1) P(S)Cell sends a PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq with scheduleChange = “start” to the SCell when activation is complete on PCell side as per (5) for one or several UEs.  
Each CA state machine enters in “WaitSCellScheduleEnableAck” state, waiting for SCell response.

On reception of the request, for each UE in the list if UE specific CSI-RS is configured for UE in Scell, SCell 5G-L2-PS completes its activation by starting the scheduling of UE specific CSI-RS transmission for Channel Acquisition.

After SCell activation (before max { rdActCaOverheatingFilterConst, 3 } CQI has been received), the number of null CQI report expected before to consider to trig RLF/OH procedure is max { rdActCaOverheatingFilterConst, 3 }.

Upon a reception of a non-null CQI, RLF/OH procedure is trigged after rdActCaOverheatingFilterConst consecutive CQI repoted with null value.

In case max { rdActCaOverheatingFilterConst, 3 } consecutive null CQI has been received after SCell activation, then RLF/OH procedure is trigged to deactivate the SCell.

(7.2) If scellDeactivationTimergNB duration is not equal to infinite, SCell starts this timer to deactivate the SCell in case there would be no data to transmit during this timer duration.

Note: If sCellActivationMethod Pcell parameters is equal to “blind” and scellDeactivationTimergNB SCell parameter is not equal to infinite, SCell cannot be activated again after any SCell deactivation (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_311), which is a possible customer choice.

(7.2.1 ) [CB008311-C] If (scellDeactivationTimergNB != infinity and NRBTS.NRCELL. sCellInactivityReleaseTimer != infinity and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod != blind)[PR708077] or ext-SCell[End PR708077]:

The SCell Inactivity Release Timer stops in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS after PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeScheduleReq with scheduleChange=start is received.[END CB008311-C]

(7.3) [CB008311-C] If NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer != infinity and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod == blind:

The SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only after receiving PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeScheduleReq with scheduleChange= ‘start’ . [END CB008311-C]

(7.4) Start Flow control on SCell side and start transmission of non-GBR data, refer to the sub-MSC.

---

##### 8.2.2.1.1.0-3 SCell activation Error cases: (ID: 11195822)

**8.2.2.1.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11195828`)

SCell activation

### Exc(2) Transmission of MAC-CE (SCell activation):

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11195835`)

SCell activation
When maximum number of HARQ retransmission is reached:

* in Blind activation method, FR2 mechanism applies: a new fresh transmission of SCell Activation MAC-CE is started (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2804\_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* [5GC001390-G, 5GC001729-C] in Buffer Based activation method, the procedure is aborted.  A new SCell activation may be decided upon next buffer status check.[End 5GC001390-G, 5GC001729-C]

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11195843`)

SCell activation

### Exc(6) Initial beam acquisition

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11195850`)

SCell activation
On reception of PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuschReceiveIndPs, a CSI report is discarded if no UE has been setup in SCell 5G-L2-PS with corresponding RNTI.

(6.1) If beam report is never received, SCell remains inactive on 5G-L2-PS perspective.

(6.2) If PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd is lost, the sequence is aborted and resumes on next CSI report with Beam information.

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11195855`)

SCell activation
Exc(7)

---

**8.2.2.1.1.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11195862`)

SCell activation

### Exc(7.1) Scell activation on SCell side

There is no mechanism to detect missing Ack for a given UE, the “start” command will be repeated at next decision time in a new PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq. In this messages, if a UE is already started on SCell 5G-L2-PS point of view, the "start" command is acked without any further processing.

[5GC001390-G, 5GC001729-C] No message supervision is needed, if PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp message is lost, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS assumes missing Ack for all corresponding UEs. [End 5GC001390-G, 5GC001729-C]

On reception of PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq with an RNTI that does not match with a UE setup in SCell 5G-L2-PS, an error is logged and a fake ACK is sent back to 5G-L2-PS to avoid any repetition.

In Beamforming case, if PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuschReceiveIndPs containing the initial beam is lost, UE cannot be activated in SCell and no Ack is sent in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp. Repeated "start" command after reception of next beam report will be successful.

---

#### 8.2.2.1.2 SCell deactivation

##### 8.2.2.1.2.1 Common procedure

###### 8.2.2.1.2.1.0-1 Common procedure Call flow: (ID: 11195882)

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11195911`)

Common procedure

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "Successful case" of CA SCell Deactivation (Multi L2-RT). The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities, including gNB\_DU, Primary L2RT, and Secondary L2RT, with specific components like PCell 5G-L1-UL & 5G-L1-DL, PCell 5G-L2-PS, PCell 5G-L2-LO, SCell 5G-L2-PS, and SCell 5G-L2-LO.
The diagram outlines a series of steps and messages exchanged during the SCell deactivation process. Key actions include:
\* **Suspending scheduling in SCell**: Initiated by the PCell.
\* **Looping through UEs**: Processing each UE in a list.
\* **Preparing SCell deactivation**: Performed in the remote SCell.
\* **Invalidating PrimaryBeamId**.
\* **Stopping UE specific CSI-RS**: For Chan Acq.
\* **Checking conditions**: `isVRLF = False`, `rrmScelIRLQStatus = good`, and `isMGapSuspend = False`.
\* **Stopping Flow Control on SCell Deactivation**.
\* **Stopping SCell deactivation Timer**: Running on the gNB.
\* **Resetting RLQ counters and `rrmScelIRLQStatus`**.
\* **Starting PUCCH Transient phase**.
\* **Starting `MacCeTrsDelay` timer**.
\* **Handling responses**: If a response is received from other UEs or SCells.
\* **Combining multiple SCell deactivate bit in MAC CE**.
\* **Re-starting `MacCeTrsDelay` timer**.
\* **`MacCeTrsDelay` timer expires**.
\* **Stopping reception of SCell CSI reports**.
\* **No PUSCH scheduling**: When possible mux with Scell CSI report.
\* **Successful DL HARQ Tx**: Triggered by MAC-CE.
\* **Stopping Transient phase**.
\* **UE Inactive state**.
The diagram also shows specific messages and their corresponding identifiers, such as:
\* `(1.1) PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeScheduleReq (list of UEs, modifType=deactivate)`
\* `5G_L2_IF_656`
\* `(1.2) Stop Flow Control on SCell Deactivation`
\* `5G_L1L2_FLOW_2358`
\* `(1.3) [Stop] scelIDeactivation TimergNB timer`
\* `(1.4) Reset RLQ counters and rrmScelIRLQStatus [5GC001390-EA]`
\* `(1.5) PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeScheduleResp (list of UEs, modifType=deactivate)`
\* `5G_L2_IF_658`
\* `(2.1) start MacCeTrsDelay timer`
\* `(2.2) combination multiple SCell deactivate bit in MAC CE`
\* `(2.3) re-start MacCeTrsDelay timer`
\* `(3) Successfull DL HARQ Tx (MAC-CE[SCell deactivation])`
\* `5G_L1L2_FLOW_259`
The diagram uses different line styles (solid, dashed, dotted) and arrow types to represent different types of messages and control flows. It also includes "Opt" and "OPT" boxes to indicate optional steps. The states of the UE are shown as "WaitSCellDeactAck state", "MacCeTrsDelay state", "WaitDeact state", and "Inactive state".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2581.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
[CNI-134375]
[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "CA SCell Deactivation (Multi L2-RT) - Successful case". It depicts the interactions between different components of a cellular network, specifically focusing on the deactivation of a Secondary Cell (SCell) in a Carrier Aggregation (CA) scenario.
The diagram shows the following components:
- **gNB\_DU**: The distributed unit of the gNB.
- **Primary L2RT**: The Layer 2 Real-Time component of the primary cell.
- **Secondary L2RT**: The Layer 2 Real-Time component of the secondary cell.
- **PCell 5G-L1-UL & 5G-L1-DL**: The Physical Layer of the primary cell for Uplink and Downlink.
- **PCell 5G-L2-PS**: The Layer 2 Protocol Stack of the primary cell.
- **PCell 5G-L2-LO**: The Layer 2 Lower Layer of the primary cell.
- **SCell 5G-L2-PS**: The Layer 2 Protocol Stack of the secondary cell.
- **SCell 5G-L2-LO**: The Layer 2 Lower Layer of the secondary cell.
- **Timer**: A timer component.
- **Ue ActiveScheduleEnabled**: Represents the UE's state where scheduling is active for the SCell.
- **Ue Inactive**: Represents the UE's state where it is inactive.
The diagram outlines a series of messages and state transitions:
1. **Initiation of SCell Deactivation**:
\* The process starts with "Ue ActiveScheduleEnabled (SCell state in Pcell)".
\* Scheduling is suspended in the SCell.
\* A message `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeScheduleReq` with `modifType=deactivate` is sent to the SCell's Layer 2.
2. **SCell Deactivation Preparation in Remote 5G-L2-PS**:
\* The remote SCell Layer 2 prepares for deactivation.
\* "BF enabled" and "Invalidate PrimaryBeamId" are performed.
\* A condition is checked: "2200 disabled (or before 1390-CB)".
\* "Stop sending UE specific CSI-RS for Chan Acq." is executed.
\* Another condition is checked: `isVRLF = False and rrmScellRLQStatus = good (1390-EA) and isMGapSuspend = False (or before 1390-EE)`.
\* A reference action `(1.2) Stop Flow Control on SCell Deactivation` is performed.
\* The `scellDeactivationTimergNB` starts running (not for an infinite value).
\* A message `(1.3) [Stop] scell Deactivation TimergNB timer` is sent.
\* RLQ counters and `rrmScellRLQStatus` are reset.
3. **SCell Deactivation Response**:
\* A response `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeScheduleResp` with `modifType=deactivate` is received, indicating the SCell deactivation is acknowledged.
\* The UE enters the "Ue Inactive" state.
4. **PUCCH Transient Phase and Timer Management**:
\* The process enters "(2) Start PUCCH Transient phase".
\* "(2.1) start MacCeTrsDelay timer" is initiated.
\* The system enters the "MacCeTrsDelay state".
\* If a response is received from other UEs or SCells (e.g., 3CC 4CC cases), `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeScheduleResp` is sent.
\* "(2.2) combination multiple SCell deactivate bit in MAC CE" is performed.
\* "(2.3) re-start MacCeTrsDelay timer" is initiated.
\* When the "MacCeTrsDelay timer expires", the system stops scheduling reception of SCell CSI reports.
\* No PUSCH scheduling is performed when possible mux with Scell CSI report.
\* The system enters the "WaitDeact state".
5. **Final Deactivation Steps**:
\* "(3) Successfull DL HARQ Tx (MAC-CE[SCell deactivation])" is performed.
\* The process enters "(4) Stop Transient phase".
\* The SCell is now in the "Inactive state".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2581.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
[End CNI-134375]

###### 8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2 Common procedure Description: (ID: 11195917)

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11195925`)

Common procedure

### (1) Suspend scheduling in SCell

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11195945`)

Common procedure
[Before CNI-134375]P(S)Cell sends to SCell a PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeScheduleReq with a list of UEs to process[CNI-134375]For each UE, which should be processed P(S)Cell sends to SCell a PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeScheduleReq[End CNI-134375]. In case modifType is equal to deactivate for a UE, SCell shall suspend the scheduling for this UE.

(1.1) If beamforming is enabled:  
On reception of PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeScheduleReq[Before CNI-134375], for each UE [CNI-134375](one msg is received per UE)[End CNI-134375], SCell 5G-L2-PS invalidates the UE Beam (may no more be accurate in case of later re-activation) and stops sending UE specific CSI-RS for Channel Acquisition when UE specific CSI-RS is configured for UE in Scell.

(1.2) A stop of Flow control is required on SCell side to stop reception of Data in L2LO and therefore suspend PDSCH scheduling.

In unikely case of race condition when SCell has detected an Overheating (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_355), a BadRLQ  or a complete overlapping between Measurement Gap and periodic CSI reports (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2878\_replaced([11123344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) since it has requested the SCell deactivation (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_336), Flow control has already been stopped so this step is not required.

(1.3) After stopping the flow Control, scellDeactivationTimergNB shall be stopped.

(1.4) Reset UE context:

discardCqiAtSCelllActivation flag is set to True (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_304).

Reset RLQ counters, rrmScellBadRLQTimes included and rrmScellRLQStatus.

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11195952`)

Common procedure

### (2) Start PUCCH Transient phase

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11195967`)

Common procedure
As for activation (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_293), this transient phase is due to the uncertainty about the transmission of periodic PUCCH after the SCell deactivation when waiting for the UE to stop the transmission of periodic SCell related CSI reports.

The one-piece “DL HARQ Tx” Sub-MSC does not allow to represent it well but Transient phase starts after sending the first SCell deactivation MAC-CE.

P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS stops scheduling reception of any SCell CSI report in PCell.

[5GC002546-B,5GC001167-H]

(2.1) P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS start delay timer to send MAC-CE to UE, to let other actived scells still can be scheduled in this period(No Ctai/Tdai changed), till DPA didn't allocate PUCCH resource for this Scell which is planned to be deactived.

P(S)Cell stops pre-allocation PUCCH for UE with this Scell in next DPA period.

(2.2)(2.3) If received Scell deactivation resp during MacCeTrsDelay Timer running, then restart the timer and combinate MAC CE Scell activation/deactivation bit map.

After delay timer expiration, continue step (3).

refer to 5G\_L2\_627\_replaced([11159271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25PqP_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC002546-B,5GC001167-H]

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11195973`)

Common procedure

### (3) Transmission of SCell deactivation MAC-CE

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12676566`)

Common procedure
The “DL HARQ Tx” Sub-MSC includes acknowledgment and possible repetitions of the MAC-CE.  
Successful MAC-CE transmission is assumed here (refer to error cases otherwise).

[PR835194] After SCell deactivation 5G-L2-PS shall clear parameters related to UE overheating status, RLQ status and measurement gap for suspended SCell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2867\_replaced\_([11123279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhsfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [End PR835194]

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11195987`)

Common procedure

### (4) End of transient phase

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11195995`)

Common procedure
The Transient phase ends 3 ms after reception of the HARQ Ack related to the SCell Deactivation MAC-CE (no timer is required to enforce this timing wen PUCCH is on FDD cell).

CA state machine enters in “Inactive” state

---

###### 8.2.2.1.2.1.0-3 Common procedure Error cases: As a general behavior if procedure fails, 5G-L2-PS resumes the procedure from failure point on next decision period (no permanant failure has been identified). (ID: 11196000)

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11196007`)

Common procedure
Exc(1)

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196014`)

Common procedure

### Exc(1.1) Suspend scheduling in SCell

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-3.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196022`)

Common procedure
There is no mechanism to detect missing Ack for a given UE, the “stop” command will be repeated at next decision time in a new PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq.

In this messages, if a UE is already stopped on SCell 5G-L2-PS point of view or unknown (already released as an example), the "stop" command is acked without any further processing.

[5GC001390-G] No message supervision is needed, if PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp message is lost, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS assumes missing Ack for all corresponding UEs. [5GC001390-G End]

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11196030`)

Common procedure

### Exc(3) Transmission of SCell Deactivation MAC-CE

---

**8.2.2.1.2.1.0-3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11196049`)

Common procedure
In case Max HARQ retransmission is reached or corresponding HARQ feedback hasn't been received from L1 (UCI considered as lost K1Max \* [Before CB009189-B] maxDlHarqTx [CB009189-B] maxDlHarqTxNum [End CB009189-B] + drxLongCycle - drxOnDurationTimer slots after MAC-CE dispatch to scheduling, K1Max being 15 as defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_277\_replaced([11514729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5En_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB009189-B] and maxDlHarqTxNum described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12742\_replaced([11185319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB009189-B]), 5G-L2-PS shall resend the Scell Deactivation MAC-CE on next decision period.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a "CA Buffer based SCell Deactivation (Multi L2-RT) - Successful case". The diagram depicts interactions between different components within a gNB\_DU (gNB Distributed Unit).
The main components are organized into two L2-RT (Layer 2 - Real Time) entities: "Primary L2RT" and "Secondary L2RT".
Under "Primary L2RT", there are two sub-components:
- PCell 5G-L2-PS
- PCell 5G-L2-LO
Under "Secondary L2RT", there are three sub-components:
- SCell 5G-L2-PS
- SCell 5G-L2-LO
- Timer
The diagram shows a timeline flowing from top to bottom. Several messages and events are depicted:
1. **Ue ActiveScheduleEnabled (SCell state in PCell)**: This event occurs in the "PCell 5G-L2-PS" lane, indicating that the UE has enabled active scheduling for the SCell, and the SCell is in the PCell state.
2. **Detect need of deactivation**: This is a trigger event, shown in pink, originating from the "PCell 5G-L2-PS" lane.
3. **Start from ActiveScheduleEnabled (SCell state in Scell)**: This event occurs in the "SCell 5G-L2-PS" lane, indicating the start of active scheduling for the SCell, with the SCell in its own state.
4. **Message (1.1) [Timeout] scellDeactivationTimergNB timer**: This message is sent from the "SCell 5G-L2-LO" lane to the "Timer" lane, indicating a timeout event for the SCell deactivation timer.
5. **Message (1.2) [Start] scellDeactivationTimergNB timer**: This message is sent from the "SCell 5G-L2-LO" lane to the "Timer" lane, initiating the SCell deactivation timer.
6. **Message (1.3) Ps PeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd (list of UEs, modifType=deactivateReq) 5G\_L2\_IF\_685**: This message is sent from the "PCell 5G-L2-LO" lane to the "SCell 5G-L2-PS" lane. It indicates a status indication from the Peer Control layer, requesting SCell deactivation for a list of UEs.
7. **Reference (Ref)**: A reference marker is shown.
8. **Message (1.4) CA SCell Deactivation (Multi L2-RT) 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_312**: This message is sent from the "SCell 5G-L2-PS" lane, referencing the flow "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_312", and signifies the actual CA SCell Deactivation process.
The diagram illustrates a scenario where the need for SCell deactivation is detected, a timer is involved, and ultimately, the CA SCell Deactivation procedure is initiated.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2604.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
Note: supported L1 variant - Loner and Loki.

###### 8.2.2.1.2.2.0-2 Buffer based SCell deactivation Description: (ID: 11196080)

**8.2.2.1.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196087`)

Buffer based SCell deactivation

### (1) SCell detects the need of deactivation

---

**8.2.2.1.2.2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196093`)

Buffer based SCell deactivation
(1.1 to 1.3) scellDeactivationTimergNB expiry

---

**8.2.2.1.2.2.0-2.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196099`)

Buffer based SCell deactivation
On scellDeactivationTimergNB expiry due to absence of data to transmit (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2733\_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SCell L2-PS a PsPeerCtrl\_ScellStatusInd sends to the PCell to request SCell deactivation (modifType equal to deactivateReq).

scellDeactivationTimergNB is restarted in case PsPeerCtrl\_ScellStatusInd would be lost (refer to error case).

---

**8.2.2.1.2.2.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11196105`)

Buffer based SCell deactivation
(1.4) Sub-MSC 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2733\_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with SCell deactivation

---

**8.2.2.1.2.2.0-2.0-1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11196118`)

Buffer based SCell deactivation
SCell waits for PCell to send back the deactivation request as part of MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_313 [CB007873-EA-UPD001] (not sent in case a SCell release is under preparation on PCell [CB007873-F]in SA / PSCell in NSA[End CB007873-F] side) [End CB007873-EA-UPD001]. The rational is to have a common scenario with future deactivation initiated by PCell (3Gpp Overheating detection as an example).

As a drawback, there could be message crossing in between but SCell deactivation is not aborted:  
- L2-LO may receive data from L2-HI:  A new SCell activation may be triggered after completion of SCell deactivation.

---

scellDeactivationTimergNB is restarted in case PsPeerCtrl\_ScellStatusInd would be lost so that PsPeerCtrl\_ScellStatusInd would be repeated (if still needed).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "CA Forwarding of CSI reports to SCell (Multi L2-RT) - Successful case". It depicts the interactions between different network entities, including 5G-UE, PCell 5G-L1-UL, PCell 5G-L2-PS, PCell 5G-L2-LO, gNB\_DU, Secondary L2RT, SCell 5G-L2-PS, and SCell 5G-L2-LO.
The diagram shows the flow of CSI (Channel State Information) reports from the UE to the network. It details various conditions and actions based on the state of the SCell and the type of CSI report.
Key elements and flows include:
\* **UE is PCell in service, SCell added and activated (or activation on-going):** This is the initial state.
\* **SCell state in PCell:** Can be `ActiveScheduleEnabled`, `WaitSCellScheduleEnableAck`, or `WaitInitBeam`.
\* **SCell state in SCell:** Can be `ActiveScheduleEnabled` or `Inactive`.
\* **PUCCH or PUSCH with CSI report:** The UE sends CSI reports via PUCCH or PUSCH.
\* **UIData\_PucchReceiveRespPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_221) or UIData\_PuschReceiveRespPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_200):** These are the messages carrying the CSI reports.
\* **Loop:** The process iterates for each CSI report on a remote SCell.
\* **ALT (Alternative) branches:**
\* **(1a) BF disabled:** If Beamforming (BF) is disabled, the CSI report is appended to a buffer.
\* **(1b) SCell state = WaitInitBeam & Beam report with DTX:** This condition handles specific scenarios for TDD and FDD.
\* **(1c) other BF case:** For other BF cases, the CSI report is discarded.
\* **opt (Optional) branches:**
\* If the SCell state is `WaitInitBeam` and a Beam report is received (for TDD or FDD), the UE enters the `WaitSCellScheduleEnableAck` state.
\* **Append CSI report in buffer:** CSI reports are buffered under certain conditions.
\* **Is at least one report to forward to SCell 'x':** A check is performed before forwarding reports.
\* **(2) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs 5G\_L2\_IF\_680 or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuschReceiveIndPs 5G\_L2\_IF\_675:** These messages indicate received CSI reports.
\* **For each CSI report related to this SCell 'x':** Another loop for processing reports.
\* **ALT branches for report processing:**
\* **BF disabled OR SCell state <> Active:** Default report processing occurs.
\* **BF enabled & SCell state = Inactive:** This condition leads to setting the initial beam.
\* **(2a) Default report processing:** Standard processing for CSI reports.
\* **(2b) Set initial Beam:** This action is taken when BF is enabled and the SCell state is inactive.
\* **Ue in ActiveScheduleDisabled state:** The UE enters this state after setting the initial beam.
The diagram also includes references to specific message identifiers like `CB008577-D` and interface identifiers like `5G_L1_IF_221`, `5G_L1_IF_200`, `5G_L2_IF_680`, and `5G_L2_IF_675`. The URL `http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v8.3.7` is present at the bottom right, indicating the tool used to generate the diagram.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01231345.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
Note: supported L1 variant - Loner and Loki.
[CB008577-D] Although FDD BF SCell has only one SSB a TCI is needed when the SCell is avtivated according to [11112694: TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE with multiple active component carriers](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA). L2-PS handle it as first TCI in the similar way as first TCI for TDD BF SCell except that it is after first valid CSI with CSI/PMI for there is  no beam report. The change is between red font of (CB008577-D) and (End CB008577). [End CB008577-D]
File "13369197\_CA Forwarding of CSI reports to SCell (Multi L2-PS).signalling" stored at:
[RAN A&S - 5GCx Spec. Repository - 8.2.2 DL Data Transfer (MAC level, inter L2-PS case) - Tree\_View](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Forms/Tree_View.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2F5Gdoc%2FAS%5FTech%5FSpec%2FDrawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G%2FUser%20Plane%2F5G%20L1%20and%20L2%20Entity%20Level%20Flows%2F8%20User%20Plane%20Data%20Transfer%2F8%2E2%20DL%20Data%20Transmission%20Scenarios%2F8%2E2%2E2%20DL%20Data%20Transfer%20%28MAC%20level%2C%20inter%20L2%2DPS%20case%29&viewid=967508b3%2D8e81%2D461c%2Db99d%2D145065cf0c1c&CID=ff728ec1%2D656f%2D4535%2D845b%2Df1ee3f84ff2b&FolderCTID=0x012000F0A0A3BA325F7648AD307E6959BA7376)

##### 8.2.2.1.3.0-2 SCell CSI report Description: (ID: 11196171)

**8.2.2.1.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196179`)

SCell CSI report

### (1) UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs or UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs

---

**8.2.2.1.3.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13369199`)

SCell CSI report
Both messages may be received in PCell slot for different UEs depending whether a PUSCH has been scheduled or not for same slot.

For non-CA UE or CSI report related to PCell, the standard processing applies, current diagram only represents processing of CSI reports related to SCell when PUCCH group is handled by P(S)Cell.

**(1a) In** non-Beamforming case, CSI reports from different UEs but received in same 5G-L1-UL message and related to the same SCell are concatenated so that they can be forwarded to this SCell in a single message.\*\*\*\*

**(1b) In Beamforming case, only DTX criteria is used to discard the initial Beam or PMI report related to SCell.**

**(1c) In Beamforming case, the P(S)Cell cannot send a SCell activation indication to SCell before initial beam [CB008577-D]for TDD or the first valid CSI with CSI/PMI for FDD SCell[End CB008577-D] is known, so the P(S)Cell need to keep track of reception of the first valid beam [CB008577-D]for TDD or the first valid CSI with CSI/PMI for FDD SCell[End CB008577-D].**

Concatenation described in **(1a) applies.**

---

**8.2.2.1.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11196190`)

SCell CSI report

### (2) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuschReceiveIndPs

###

---

**8.2.2.1.3.0-2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13369221`)

SCell CSI report
If the number of CSI reports exceeds maximum allowed per PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs (5G\_L2\_IF\_680\_replaced([10979816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VdxGvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the remaining CSI reports shall be sent in the subsequent message(s).

For each UE:

**(2a) In non-Beamforming case, the default processing of CSI reports for Channel Acquisition applies to SCell.**

In Beamforming case, when initial beam has been set, the default processing of CSI reports for Channel Acquisition or Beam update applies to SCell.

**(2b) In Beamforming case, when initial beam has not been set during SCell activation, the initial beam is set on reception of the first non DTX Beam report [CB008577-D]for TDD or the first nonDTX CSI with CQI/PMI for FDD SCell with dlMimoMode=80[End CB008577-D].**

Note: There is no check on sinr measurement (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1992\_replaced([11112073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for validity of the first beam.

CSI reports for Channel Acquisition received before initial beam is set are discarded as UE cannot report a valid measurement (and SCell 5G-L2-PS cannot schedule transmission of UE specific CSI-RS **that are used when UE specific CSI-RS is configured for UE in Scell). This discard is important to avoid fake virtual RLF or Overheating detection during SCell activation (refer to discardCqiAtSCelllActivation flag in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_304).**

---

MSC: CA SCell scheduling suspend on Virtual RLF or Over-heating detection (Multi L2-RT)
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the process of CA SCell scheduling suspension on Virtual RLF or Overheating detection in a Multi L2-RT system.
The flowchart is organized into columns representing different components: Primary L2RT, Secondary L2RT, and gNB\_DU. Within these columns, specific entities like PCell, SCell, and Timer are depicted.
The process begins with the UE being in PCell service, with SCell added and activated. The UE's state is described as "ActiveScheduleEnabled" and can transition to "WaitTciStateAck" or "ActiveSuspended".
A key part of the flowchart involves the forwarding of CSI reports. When a CSI report with an invalid CQI-0 is received, it triggers a loop that processes each CSI report. Inside this loop, there's an optional step (OPT) where a condition "is MGapSuspend = False" is checked. If this condition is met, the system proceeds to detect vRLF/OH, setting "is VRLF = True" and disabling RLQ checking.
Another optional step checks if "rrm ScellIRLQStatus = good". If true, it leads to stopping flow control. Concurrently, the system continues scheduling PUCCH reception for SCell CSI reports and sending UE-specific CSI-RS.
Further down, another optional step initiates a "scellDeactivationTimergNB" running for a finite value, followed by stopping the timer. The final state shown is "ActiveSuspended".
A note at the bottom indicates that the PCell is not aware of the PDSCH scheduling suspend in SCell.
The flowchart uses various shapes and connectors to represent different actions, conditions, and data flows. Rectangular boxes represent processes or states, diamonds represent decisions or conditions, and arrows indicate the flow of control. Labels and references like "Ref", "LOOP", "OPT", and specific flow identifiers (e.g., "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_345") provide additional context.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2628.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
File "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_356\_CA SCell scheduling suspend on vRLF or OH detection (Multi L2-RT).signalling" stored at:

###### 8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2 SCell scheduling Suspend Description: (ID: 11196247)

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196252`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
(1) Reception of CSI reports for Channel acquisition in SCell

---

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11196265`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
As described in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_345, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS periodically receives CQI report from UE and forwards them to  SCell 5G-L2-PS either in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuschReceiveIndPs.

[CB007873-EA][CB007873-F]Note that this sequence cannot take place when SCell release has been started as forwarding of SCell CSI report is disabled at that time. [End CB007873-F][End CB007873-EA]

---

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11196272`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
(2) Suspend PDSCH scheduling in SCell

---

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196278`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
(2.1) Detect Virtual RLF or Overheating

---

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196284`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
SCell 5G-L2-PS detects a Virtual RLF or an overheating on reception of rdActCAOverheatingFilterConst consecutive invalid CQI equal to 0. [5GC001390-EE] It does not apply if SCell scheduling is already suspended due overlapping between Measurement Gaps and periodic CSI reports (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2878\_replaced([11123344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End 5GC001390-EE]

Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2871\_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detection of Overheating criteria and 5G\_L2\_1293\_replaced([11184543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6NvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_1293\_replaced([11184543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6NvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) respectively for rdEnableCAOverheatingMonitor and rdActCAOverheatingFilterConst parameters.

[5GC001390-EA] When isVRLF is equal to True, RLQ checking for SCell scheduling suspend/resume or Deactivate is disabled (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_411). [End 5GC001390-EA]

Note that SCell 5G-L2-PS does not make difference between Pre-3GPP Overheating detection and Virtual RLF in SCell.

---

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11196291`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
(2.2) Stop Flow control

---

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196298`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
SCell remains activated but Stop the flow control procedure, flushes RLC PDU buffers (DL Data and Status not yet transmitted to the UE) and stops pending HARQ retransmission to suspend PDSCH scheduling in SCell (same sequence as before SCell Deactivation) as UE is no more able to decode it.

[5GC001390-EA] This sequence is not required when PDSCH scheduling in SCell has been already suspended for bad RLQ reason. [End 5GC001390-EA]

---

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11196305`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
(2.3) and Stop inactivity timer

---

**8.2.2.1.4.1.0-2.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11196316`)

SCell scheduling Suspend
P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall keep on scheduling of PUCCH reception for SCell CSI-RS reports to make sure SCell can detect Overheating recovery. Therefore, when Beamforming is enabled [Before CB008534-C] and 5GC002200 is disabled[END CB008534-C][CB008534-C]and UE specific CSI-RS is configured for UE in Scell[END CB008534-C], SCell 5G-L2-PS shall keep on scheduling of UE-specific CSI-RS for Channel Acquisition and stop the inactivity timer as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2733\_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to avoid Scell deactivation.

Note that UE-specific CSI-RS (for Channel Acquisition) may be transmitted in an invalid beam but it has no consequences has beam recovery will take place before any SCell PDSCH scheduling as part of recovery procedure.

This sequence is not required when PDSCH scheduling in SCell has been already suspended for bad RLQ reason.

---
