MSC: CA Resume scheduling in SCell on recovery from Over-heating or Virtual RLF
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of resuming SCell scheduling after recovery from overheating or a virtual RLF in a successful case. The diagram depicts interactions between different components, including the UE, gNB\_DU, Primary L2RT, and Secondary L2RT.
The diagram is structured with swimlanes representing these components. The Primary L2RT has sub-components: PCell 5G-L1-UL, PCell 5G-L2-PS, and PCell 5G-L2-LO. The Secondary L2RT has sub-components: SCell 5G-L2-PS, SCell 5G-L2-LO, and Timer.
The scenario begins with the UE in PCell service, with SCell added and activated, but SCell PDSCH scheduling is suspended due to Overheating (OH). The SCell state is initially "ActiveSuspended".
A "LOOP: (Recovery detection)" is initiated. Within this loop, a condition "vRLF = True" is checked. If true, an "OPT: (Beam update or Recovery)" is performed, leading to "BF enabled".
Following this, a reference action "(1) SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state (Multi L2-RT)" (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_390) is executed. Subsequently, another reference action "(2.1) Successful Forwarding of CSI reports to SCell (CQI report)" (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_345) occurs.
A check for "(2.2) Check vRLF/OH recovery" is performed. If recovery is detected and the SCell is not in "WaitTciStateAck", a "(2.3) Context Reset" is triggered. This reset involves setting "vRLF = False", resetting the LA context, and resetting RLQ counters. Finally, "Restart RLQ checking [1390-EA]" is initiated.
The diagram then transitions to "Resume PD SCH scheduling".
An "ALT:" (alternative) path is shown, where "rmmScelIRLQStatus = good (or before 1390-EA)". Under this condition, a reference action "(3.1) Start Flow Control" (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_507) is executed.
Another "OPT:" (optional) path is presented, checking if "scellDeactivationTimergNB duration is not equal to infinite". If this is true, "(3.2) [Start] scellDeactivation TimergNB timer" is initiated, leading to the "ActiveScheduleEnabled" state.
If "rmmScelIRLQStatus = bad", a reference action "(3.3) Resume scheduling on recovery from Bad RLQ" (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_428) is performed.
A separate message box indicates that "PCell is not aware of PD SCH scheduling resume in SCell".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2644.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
File "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_371\_Resume scheduling in SCell on recovery from OH or vRLF.signalling" stored at:

**8.2.2.1.4.2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196381`)

(2.1 and 2.2) Detect recovery on reception of SCell CSI reports for Channel acquisition

**8.2.2.1.4.2.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11196395`)

SCell scheduling Resume
As described in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_345, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS periodically receives CQI report from UE and forwards them to  SCell 5G-L2-PS either in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs or PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuschReceiveIndPs.

SCell 5G-L2-PS detects recovery on reception of rdDeactCAOverheatingFilterConst consecutive valid CQI reports i.e. different than CQI-0 (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2874\_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for principle, 5G\_L2\_1293\_replaced([11184543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6NvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_1295\_replaced([11184553](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6OPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for parameters).

No detection takes place when:

* MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_390 is not complete (SCell still in WaitTciAck state)r
* [CB007873-EA] a SCell release is under preparation on PCell [CB007873-F]in SA / PSCell in NSA[End CB007873-F] side (SCell not informed before SCell release execution, refer to TBD) as forwarding of SCell CSI report forwarding is disabled at that time. [End CB007873-EA]

**8.2.2.1.4.2.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11196403`)

SCell scheduling Resume
(2.3) UE Context reset

**8.2.2.1.4.2.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196409`)

SCell scheduling Resume
isVRLF flag is set to False. [5GC001390-EA] It enables again RLQ checking for SCell scheduling suspend/resume or Deactivate (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_411). [End 5GC001390-EA]

Additionnaly:

* Link adaptation is reset to initial MCS.
* [5GC001390-EA] RLQ counters (except rrmScellBadRLQTimes) are reset so that a new RLQ evaluation period starts. If a bad rrmScellRLQStatus  (MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_407) has triggered PDSCH scheduling suspension before detection of Overheating or Virtual RLF, a good RLQ evaluation is required to resume PDSCH scheduling in SCell (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_428). [End 5GC001390-EA]

**8.2.2.1.4.2.0-2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11196448`)

(3.3) Check recovery from Bad RLQ

---

**8.2.2.1.4.2.0-2.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11196456`)

SCell scheduling Resume
In case a Bad RLQ has been detected before Virtual RLF / Overheating, a recovery from bad RLQ is additionaly required to resume PDSCH scheduling in SCell.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state" scenario, specifically the "Successful case".
The diagram depicts interactions between different components of a gNB\_DU (gNodeB Distributed Unit), including Primary L2RT (Layer 2 Relay) and Secondary L2RT. Within these L2RTs, there are specific cells like PCell 5G-L1-UL, PCell 5G-L2-PS, PCell 5G-L2-LO, SCell 5G-L1-UL, SCell 5G-L1-DL, and SCell 5G-L2-PS.
The scenario begins with a UE (User Equipment) being in PCell service, with SCell added and activated, but SCell PDSCH (Physical Downlink Shared Channel) scheduling suspended. The SCell state in PCell is "ActiveScheduleEnabled", while the SCell state in SCell is "ActiveSuspended".
The "Beam recovery" process is initiated.
Here's a breakdown of the sequence of events:
1. **(1.1) Successfull Forwarding of CSI reports to SCell (with non DTX Beam report)**: This is a reference event, indicated by a "Ref" box, and is associated with the flow "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_345".
2. **(1.2) Beam update**: This event is triggered when the "beam has changed and vRLF = True or rrmScelIRLQStatus = bad (or before 1390-EA)".
3. **(1.3) PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd(list of UE, modifType=sendTciPdcchReq, macCePayload)**: This message is sent with the flow "5G\_L2\_IF\_685".
4. **(1.4) Successfull DL HARQ Tx MAC-CE [ TCI state Indication for Ue-specific PDCCH ]**: This is another reference event, associated with the flow "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_259".
5. **WaitTciStateAck state**: This state is entered.
6. **(1.5) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeScheduleReq (list of UE, modifType=sendTciPdcchAck)**: This message is sent with the flow "5G\_L2\_IF\_656".
7. **ActiveSuspended**: The SCell state in SCell becomes "ActiveSuspended".
8. **(1.6) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeScheduleResp (list of UEs, modifType=sendTciPdcchAck)**: This response message is sent with the flow "5G\_L2\_IF\_658".
The diagram uses vertical lines to represent lifelines of different components and horizontal arrows to indicate messages exchanged between them. The "OPT" section indicates optional steps or conditions.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2664.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
File "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_391\_SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state.signalling" stored at:

###### 8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2 SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state Description: (ID: 11196490)

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196496`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
Precondition

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196502`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
This procedure only applies when PDSCH scheduling is suspended in SCell as "MAC-CE TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH" would be transmitted on SCell PDSCH otherwise.

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11196508`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
(1) Beam update recovery

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196514`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
(1.1 and 1.2) Beam update

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196522`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
When UE is in Overheating [5GC001390-EA] or SCell 5G-L2-PS has detected a Bad RLQ [End 5GC001390-EA], UE keeps reporting the best beams so SCell 5G-L2-PS applies standard Beam selection.

In Virtual RLF condition a dummy beam is reported but lowest RSRP ensures that beam report is discarded. If UE recovers, UE reports a valid beam before SCell 5G-L2-PS detects the recovery (MAC-CE TCI State Indication for UE specific PDCCH required to receive a valid CQI report) and standard Beam selection applies.

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11196528`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
(1.3 to 1.4) Send MAC-CE TCI State Indication over PCell

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196534`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
The "MAC-CE TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH" shall be sent over PCell when scheduling of SCell PDSCH is suspended.

So, SCell 5G-L2-PS sends information to build this MAC-CE to P(S)Cell in PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd message with modif Type equal to sendTciPdcchReq.

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11196541`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
(1.5) Send MAC-CE TCI State Indication over PCell

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11196548`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
A PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq with modifType equal to sendTciPdcchAck is sent back to the SCell 5G-L2-PS to acknowledge the transmission of the MAC-CE.

This acknowledgement is mandatory, sheduling cannot resume when UE is in WaitTciStateAck state.

---

###### 8.2.2.1.4.3.0-3 SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state Error cases: (ID: 11196555)

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11196561`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
Exc(1) TCI State Indication MAC-CE

---

**8.2.2.1.4.3.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196568`)

SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state
In case the PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd or the PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq is lost, the sequence is aborted and resumes on reception of next SCell CSI report with Beam information.

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of suspending or deactivating a Secondary Cell (SCell) based on bad Radio Link Quality (RLQ) detection in a Multi L2-RT (Layer 2 - Radio Transmission) system. The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities, including the gNB\_DU (gNodeB Distributed Unit), Primary L2RT, and Secondary L2RT, which comprises SCell 5G-L1-UL, SCell 5G-L1-DL, SCell 5G-L2-PS, and SCell 5G-L2-LO Timer.
The diagram outlines a series of steps and conditions that lead to the deactivation of an SCell. Key events include:
\* **Periodic Check for this UE:** The process begins with a periodic check for the UE.
\* **UE is PCell in service, SCell added and activated:** This indicates the initial state where the UE is operational with both Primary Cell (PCell) and Secondary Cell (SCell).
\* **Successful Forwarding of CSI reports to SCell:** The diagram shows the successful forwarding of Channel State Information (CSI) reports from the UE to the SCell.
\* **Update Bad & Good RLQ counters:** The system updates counters based on the received CSI reports and a proposed MCS (Modulation and Coding Scheme).
\* **SCell Channel Estimation Period:** The process reaches the end of the SCell channel estimation period.
\* **SCell RLQ Status:** The status of the SCell RLQ is determined, and if it's bad, the RLQ counters are reset.
\* **SCell RLQ Status has changed from good to bad:** This condition triggers further actions.
\* **Stop Flow Control:** Flow control is stopped for the SCell.
\* **Keep on scheduling PUCCH reception for SCell CSI report:** The system continues to schedule PUCCH reception for SCell CSI reports.
\* **Keep on sending UE specific CSI-RS:** The system continues to send UE-specific CSI-RS.
\* **SCell Deactivation Timer:** A timer related to SCell deactivation is initiated or managed.
\* **NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB and NRCELLsCellInactivityReleaseTimer:** These timers are checked for their values.
\* **Start sCellInactivityRelease Timer:** The inactivity release timer for the SCell is started.
\* **ActiveSuspended:** The SCell enters an "ActiveSuspended" state.
\* **SCell Bad RLQ Times:** A counter for bad RLQ times is incremented.
\* **SCell Bad RLQ Times >= sCellDeactivationBadRiq Count:** This condition checks if the number of bad RLQ times exceeds a threshold.
\* **Stop sCellInactivity Release Timer:** The inactivity release timer is stopped.
\* **SCell Status Ind:** A status indication is sent regarding the SCell.
\* **SCell Deactivation:** The SCell is ultimately deactivated.
The diagram uses different colored boxes to represent messages and states:
\* **White boxes:** Represent messages or actions.
\* **Gray boxes:** Represent conditions or states.
\* **Green boxes:** Represent specific messages or events, often with associated timer values or conditions.
\* **Dashed boxes:** Indicate logical groupings of components.

###### 8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2 SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate Description: (ID: 11196620)

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196627`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(1) Periodic Monitoring of Channel Quality in Scell

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196633`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(1.1) CQI computation

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196641`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
PDSCH scheduling in SCell is not suspended due to Overheating, vRLF [5GC001390-EE] or permanent collision between CSI-RS/Report and Measurement Gap [End 5GC001390-EE]. So SCell 5G-L2-PS periodically performs checks as per timing in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2778\_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

A valid CQI has been previously reported as part of Inner-loop Link adaptation and an adjustment has possibly been made according to BLER (Outer-loop). Thus, a valid proposedMCS is available as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3045\_replaced([11125301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqt5svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11196647`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(1.2) RLQ counter update on periodic check

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196653`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
On every check, if proposed MCS is valid, either Good or Bad RLQ counter is incremented as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2764\_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) depending on MCS quality thresholds.

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11196660`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(2) rrmScellRLQStatus update

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196667`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
If number of valid checks multiplied by checking periodicity is greater or equal than sCellChannelEstimationPeriod, rrmScellRLQStatus (good or bad) is computed as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2767\_replaced([11121583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), depending on the percentage of bad RLQ periods.

RLQ counters are reset before starting a new evaluation.

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11196673`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(3) Suspend PDSCH scheduling on transition from Good to Bad RLQ

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11196678`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(3.1) Stop Flow control

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196685`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
The Stop flow control procedure suspends PDSCH scheduling in SCell.

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11196692`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(3.2) Stop inactivity timer

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11196699`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
scellDeactivationTimergNB timer is stopped to avoid Buffer based SCell deactivation when PDSCH scheduling is suspended in SCell.

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11196705`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(3.3) Start inactivity release timer

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11196712`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
Bad RLQ trigger UE enter suspend state, the SCell traffic stopped,

If (NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB = infinity and NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer != infinity), The SCell Inactivity Release Timer shall be starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS.

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11196719`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
(4) Persistent SCell deactivation

---

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11196733`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
As per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2774\_replaced([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), rrmScellBadRLQTimes counts the number of consecutives rrmScellRLQStatus evaluation equal to bad.

If sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount threshold is not equal to infinite and rrmScellBadRLQTimes is greater or equal than this value, SCell 5G-L2-PS sends a PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd message to the PCell with modifType equal to “persistentDeactivateReq”.

PCell 5G-L2-PS behaviour is same as for “deactivateReq” buffer-based deactivation in MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_313 except that PCell shall not evaluate this SCell for buffer-based activation anymore until SCell release.

[CB008311-C] (4.2.0) If SCell Inactivity Release Timer is running,  stop it before SCell 5G-L2-PS sends PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd with modifType == 'persistentDeactivateReq' to PCell 5G-L2-PS.

(4.2.1) If NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq is set to ‘enabled\_Fr1’ :

PCell 5G-L2-PS sends PsUser\_SCellReleaseConditionMetInd message with inactiveReason = 'bad\_RLQ' to 5G-L3-CPRT.

[END CB008311-C]

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
Exc(4) Persistent SCell deactivation

**8.2.2.1.5.1.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11196753`)

SCell Scheduling Suspend or Deactivate
In case PsPeerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd message would be lost, the procedure resumes on next check on rrmScellBadRLQTimes.

MSC: CA SCell scheduling resume on Bad RLQ detection (Multi L2-RT)
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the process of "Resume scheduling in SCell on recovery from Bad RLQ" in a successful case. The flowchart is organized into several sections, including "Primary L2RT", "Secondary L2RT", and "gNB\_DU".
The flowchart begins with the UE being in PCell service, with SCell added and activated, but SCell PD SCH scheduling suspended due to Bad RLQ (No Over-Heating or Measurement Gap collision). The SCell state is initially "ActiveSuspended".
The process then enters a "LOOP: (Recovery detection)" phase. Within this loop, there's an "OPT: (Beam update)" section. If "BF enabled", a reference step "(1.1) SCell Beam update or recovery in suspended state (Multi L2-RT)" is performed, followed by another reference step "(1.2) Successful Forwarding of CSI reports to SCell (CQI report)".
Following this, a "Periodic Check for this UE" is conducted. If "proposedMCS is valid and", the process proceeds to "(2) Update Bad & Good RLQ counters according to proposedMCS", incrementing "rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ".
Another "OPT" block checks if the "reach end of sCellChannelEstimationPeriod" and if the "SCell state not WaitTciStateAck". If these conditions are met, step "(3) rrmScelIRLQStatus = f (% of bad MCS)" is executed, which involves resetting RLQ counters and "rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ".
The flowchart then moves to the "Resume PD SCH scheduling" section. This section includes "(4.1) Context Reset", setting "rrmScellBadRLQTimes = 0". A "Start Flow control" is initiated, with a reference to "(4.2) Start Flow Control".
Finally, another "OPT" block checks if "scellDeactivationTimergNB duration is not equal to infinite". If true, it triggers "(4.3) [Start] scellDeactivationTimergNB timer", leading to the SCell state becoming "ActiveScheduleEnabled". The flowchart concludes with a note that "PCell is not aware of PD SCH scheduling resume in SCell".
The flowchart uses various shapes to represent different elements:
- Rectangles with rounded corners represent states or conditions (e.g., "ActiveScheduleEnabled", "ActiveSuspended").
- Rectangles represent processes or actions (e.g., "Update Bad & Good RLQ counters according to proposedMCS").
- Diamonds represent optional steps or decision points (labeled "OPT").
- Arrows indicate the flow of control.
- Boxes with "Ref" indicate referenced procedures.
- Dashed lines delineate logical groupings of components (e.g., "gNB\_DU").[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2707.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

In case a beam update is on going, rrmScellRLQStatus evaluation is postponed until UE has switched to the new beam (i.e. PCell 5G-L2-PS has confirmed reception of acknowledgement for MAC-CE TCI State Indication for user-specific PDCCH, refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_390) so that PDSCH transmission does not resume on the wrong beam.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of ext-Scell deactivation and reactivation due to synchronization status changes. The diagram is divided into two main sections: "prime-gNB" and "ext-gNB". Each section further breaks down into components like "5G-CP-RT" and "PCell's 5G-L2-PS" or "ext-SCell's 5G-L2-PS".
The diagram depicts several interactions:
**Alt (Alternative) Flow:**
\* **(1.1) If Synchronization status change on prime-gNB and PCell has inter-gNB CA relation:** This is a conditional statement indicating a trigger for the subsequent actions.
\* **(1.2) PsCell\_SyncStatusInd syncStatus = OutOfSync/InSync:** A message is sent from 5G-CP-RT to PCell's 5G-L2-PS, indicating a change in synchronization status (either OutOfSync or InSync).
\* **(2.1) If Synchronization status change on ext-gNB and ext-SCell has inter-gNB CA relation:** Another conditional statement, this time related to the ext-gNB.
\* **(2.2) PsCell\_SyncStatusInd syncStatus = OutOfSync / InSync:** A message is sent from 5G-CP-RT to ext-SCell's 5G-L2-PS, indicating a synchronization status change.
\* **(2.3) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellMeasurementRep syncStatus = OutOfSync/InSync:** A message is sent from ext-SCell's 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT, reporting measurement results related to synchronization status.
**Loop Flow:**
\* **(3) For each UE with inter-gNB CA relation:** This indicates that the following steps are performed for every User Equipment (UE) that has an inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation (CA) relation.
\* **(4) PsPeerCtrl\_SCellUeSchedulingReq modifType = deactivateExtScellOutOfSync/start:** A request is sent to the UE to modify its scheduling. The `modifType` can be "deactivateExtScellOutOfSync" or "start".
\* **(5) PsPeerCtrl\_SCellUeSchedulingResp modifType = deactivateExtScellOutOfSync / start:** A response is received from the UE, confirming the scheduling modification. The `modifType` is the same as in the request.
The overall diagram illustrates how synchronization status changes in either the prime-gNB or ext-gNB can trigger deactivation or reactivation of ext-Scells, and how this process involves communication between different network components and the UE.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2729.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating DL HARQ Tx (Multi L2-PS) PDSCH scheduling over two different L2-PS instances synchronized using the PsPeerCtrl interface. The diagram depicts interactions between a 5G-UE, PCell 5G-L1-UL, PCell 5G-L1-DL, PCell 5G-L2-PS, PCell 5G-L2-LO, SCell 5G-L1-DL, SCell 5G-L2-PS, and SCell 5G-L2-LO, all under the gNB DU.
The diagram is divided into several sections, representing different functionalities and communication flows.
**Key components and interactions:**
\* **5G-UE:** Represents the User Equipment.
\* **PCell 5G-L1-UL/DL:** Primary Cell Layer 1 User Plane/Downlink.
\* **PCell 5G-L2-PS/LO:** Primary Cell Layer 2 Packet Switched/Logical Object.
\* **SCell 5G-L1-DL:** Secondary Cell Layer 1 Downlink.
\* **SCell 5G-L2-PS/LO:** Secondary Cell Layer 2 Packet Switched/Logical Object.
\* **gNB DU:** gNodeB Distributed Unit.
\* **Primary L2RT & Secondary L2RT:** Indicate the primary and secondary Layer 2 Real-Time components.
**Main Flows:**
1. **Primary L2RT Scheduling:**
\* The diagram starts with a loop on SCell slots 'm' associated with the same Pucch SlotPCell.
\* The PCell 5G-L2-PS component is involved in scheduling.
\* It involves messages like `DIData_PdcchSendReq`, `DIData_PdschSendReq`, `LoCtrl_PduMuxReq`, and `DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq`.
\* A key message is `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingInd` which carries information about Pucch SlotPCell, rnti, pucch ResourceId, and numHarqANBits.
2. **Secondary L2RT Scheduling (Loop on CA UEs):**
\* This section deals with Carrier Aggregation (CA) UEs scheduled in a remote SCell.
\* It involves updating expected PUCCH feedback in the UE DB based on UE scheduling in SCell.
\* Messages include `PsPeerCtrl_PoellStatusInd` to update PCell DRX status.
\* Similar to the primary flow, it involves `DIData_PdachSendReq`, `DIData_PdschSendReq`, `LoCtrl_PduMuxReq`, and `DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq`.
3. **UCI sent on PCell's PUCCH/PUSCH:**
\* This section details the transmission of Uplink Control Information (UCI) on PCell's PUCCH and PUSCH.
\* It involves messages like `UIData_PucchReceiveReq`, `UIData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD`, `UIData_PuschReceiveReq`, and `UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD`.
\* Crucially, it shows DL HARQ Feedback of all CCs in joint-UCI via the 5G-L1-UL of the UE's PCell.
\* It also indicates HARQ Feedback related to SCell only, with the message `PsPeerCtrl_ScellPuXchReceiveInd HarqD`.
4. **CSI Report Forwarding:**
\* The diagram shows that UCI contains CSI reports.
\* There's a step for "Forwarding of CSI reports to SCell" with the message `5G_L1L2_FLOW_345`.
5. **HARQ Retransmission:**
\* A note at the bottom explains that HARQ retransmission is sent via the same 5G-L2-PS and 5G-L1 where the original transmission took place, until HARQ ACK is received or `numOfTx` reaches `maxDIHarqTx`. This sequence is also applicable to retransmissions.
The diagram uses different arrow styles and labels to represent the flow of messages and control signals between the various network entities. Shaded areas indicate specific operational contexts or loops. The use of "Opt" suggests optional steps or conditions. "Alt" indicates alternative paths. "Ref" points to a reference.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2753.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
Note: supported L1 variant - Loner and Loki.
 
File "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_452\_DL HARQ Tx (Multi L2-PS).signalling" stored at:
[End CNI-136896-A]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the DL HARQ Transmission (Multi L2-PS) process, specifically focusing on PDSCH scheduling synchronized using a PsPeerCtrl interface. The diagram depicts interactions between a 5G-UE, PCell (Primary Cell) and SCell (Secondary Cell) across different L2-PS and L2-LO layers, as well as the gNB-DU (gNodeB Distributed Unit).
The diagram is structured with vertical lifelines representing the different entities and horizontal arrows indicating messages exchanged between them. The messages are numbered and include details about the sender, receiver, message name, and associated interface/protocol information.
Key processes and messages shown include:
\* **Scheduling and Feedback:** The diagram shows scheduling decisions for PDCCH and PDSCH, and the subsequent feedback mechanisms. This includes messages like `DIData_PdcchSendReq`, `DIData_PdschSendReq`, and `DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq`.
\* **UE State and Scheduling Information:** Messages like `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingind` and `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUpdateind` are used to convey scheduling information and update the UE's state.
\* **PUCCH and PUSCH Feedback:** The diagram details the transmission of UCI (Uplink Control Information) on PUCCH and PUSCH, including `UIData_PucchReceiveReq`, `UIData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD`, `UIData_PuschReceiveReq`, and `UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD`.
\* **HARQ Feedback:** DL HARQ feedback is exchanged, with messages like `PsPeerCtrl_ScellPuXchReceivedindHarqD` indicating HARQ feedback related to SCell only or joint-UCI.
\* **CSI Reports:** The forwarding of CSI (Channel State Information) reports is also depicted.
\* **DRX Realignments:** The diagram mentions UE scheduling in SCell or the need for DRX realignment.
\* **HARQ Retransmissions:** A note at the bottom explains that HARQ retransmissions follow the same path as the original transmission until HARQ ACK is received or the maximum number of transmissions is reached.
The diagram is divided into sections representing different stages or types of interactions, with shaded areas grouping related messages. The interface information, such as `5G_L1_IF_XX` and `5G_L2_IF_XX`, indicates the specific layers and interfaces involved in the communication.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2756.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

#### 8.2.2.2.0-2 DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA) Description: (ID: 11197119)

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197124`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)

### (1) PDSCH Scheduling in a remote SCell: loop on SCell slots 'm' associated to same PUCCH

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13351985`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
Diagram represents current use case with a single remote SCell case but in case there would be several remote SCells possibly on different cores or L2RT instances, the sequence would be repeated for each SCell.

As PUCCH resource is handled by P(S)Cell, K1Scell‘s unit refers to PCell numerology. As a consequence, when SCell’s SCS is greater than P(S)Cell’s one, several consecutives SCell slots ‘m’ can schedule a PDSCH using a common PUCCH resource in PCell.

The UE DB is updated with HARQ feedback parameters related this PUCCH at a common index equal to the PucchSlotPCell translated in SCell numerology (refer to example below).

The parameters are the following: Pucch resource identifier, harqProcessIndex[] and harqANBits (bitmap indicates scheduled PDSCHs over these slots ‘m’).

**FDD + FR1 TDD CA use case:Although a unique K1TDD value is used, two consecutives DL TDD slots can be associated to the same PucchSlotPCell = K1TDD + slot/2.**

Expected HARQ feedback parameters are stored in UE DB at common index equal to PucchSlotSCell = 2\* PucchSlotPCell.

Exchanged messages (1.1) to (1.6) are the same as for single L2-PS use case, refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_260 for more information.

**FR1 TDD + FDD CA use case:**

Although a unique K1TDD value is used, one SCell FDD slot slot\_scell can be mapped to two consecutives P(s)Cell TDD slots slot\_pcell\_1 = slot\_scell*2 and  slot\_pcell\_2 = slot\_scell*2 + 1, and K1TDD is the slot distance between slot\_pcell\_2 and PUCCH/PUSCH slot holding DL HARQ A/N feedback: PucchSlotPCell = K1TDD + slot\_pcell\_2 = K1TDD + slot\_scell\*2 + 1.

Expected HARQ feedback parameters are stored in UE DB at common index equal to PucchSlotSCell = (PucchSlotPCell **+ 1) / 2. Rational: to assure HARQ management works well on SCell side, we must avoid the situation that more than one PCell PUCCH slots are mapped to same SCell PUCCH slot. For all supported TDD FR1 frame structures (see 5G\_UP\_54\_replaced([11346921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubIls_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), at most two PUCCH slots are adjacently located where leading slot is always an even one, and it is easy to know that ‘PucchSlotSCell = (PucchSlotPCell** + 1) / 2’ formula works well in avoiding the situation mentioned, so we adopted it for simplicity consideration. But, to be noted current approach may not be extensible for new frame structure and/or new CA variant, as the result, a new formula or approach must be considered if the situation of two TDD PUCCH slots mapped to one FDD SCell PUCCH slot does not stand anymore for some reason in the future.\*\*\*\*

Exchanged messages (1.1) to (1.6) are the same as for single L2-PS use case, refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_260 for more information.

[Before CNI-136896-A]

If DPA is NOT enabled:

In **5GC1390-C Pipeline solution, SCell allocates a PUCCH resource to each scheduled UEs before P(S)Cell scheduling for both slots and reports allocated list to P(S)Cell before PDSCH scheduling in PCell (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_485 for detailed explanation on timings).  
Allocated resource is either the periodic PUCCH F3 (Resource Set 2) matching with the CSI report resource in case such report is expected in that slot (simultaneousHarqAckCsi = true, otherwise UE is not scheduled) or a F1 (Resource Set 0) otherwise.**

If DPA is enabled:

[End CNI-136896-A]

SCell only use PUCCH resource pre-allocated by DPA, P(S)Cell use PUCCH resource pre-allocated by DPA or allocate PUCCH resource just as non-CA UE if no DPA allocation for the UE.

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11197147`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)

### (1.7)  Update PUCCH context in P(S)Cell according to UE scheduling in SCell

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11197165`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
SCell provides P(S)Cell with the list of scheduled UE (RNTI,  harqANBits), so that it can update its PUCCH context for that PucchSlotPCell with the total number of expected HARQ AN bits for P(S)Cell and SCell(s) (refer to 5G\_L2\_637\_replaced([11160099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25VJy_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[Before CB006137-AC]This information is also used to accurately update DRX state in both Uplink and Downlink P(S)Cell L2-PS according to PDSCH scheduling that takes place in remote SCell(s) (refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_479 for more information). [End CB006137-AC]

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11197170`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
(1.8) Update of Normalized PRB number and K1 list of serving cell

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11197174`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
In case of SCell reconfiguration when numPdschPrbInSsbSlots OR numPdschPrbInTrsSlots will change, SCell provides to P(S)Cell  the Normalized PRB number (normPrbSizeDl) and K1 list of serving cell (k1ValueInOnePeriod) within PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUpdateInd (refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_6856\_replaced([10979640](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vci-Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

### (2)  PDSCH Scheduling in L2-PS instance handling the P(S)Cell

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11197185`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)

### (2.1)  Check DRX inactivity timer expiries for P(S)Cell and SCell in DL

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11197190`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS checks inactivity timer expiries in DL and UL DRX state from previous slot.

Please refer to dedicated diagram in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_479 for more information on DRX notifications sent to SCell.

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11197195`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)

### (2.2 to 2.7)  Update PUSCH scheduler with t-DAI according to scheduling in P(S)Cell and SCell

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197201`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
There is no change compared to HARQ management for CA with single L2-PS instance (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_260).

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)

### (2.8)  Update PUSCH scheduler with t-DAI according to scheduling in P(S)Cell and SCell

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-4.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `13351986`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
[Before CNI-136896-A]

if DPA is NOT enabled:

There is no change compared to HARQ management for CA with single L2-PS instance (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_260).

Note: In 5GC1390-C Pipeline solution, Downlink P(S)Cell L2-PS has already received scheduling information from remote SCell so current DL to UL intra-sched containing t-DAI and DL DRX information  is used without any change.

if DPA is enabled:

{

[End CNI-136896-A]

**if** actK1OptForDPA**(it is false, 5G\_L2\_3076\_replaced([11141553](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23pHvvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** is NOT enabled:***\****\*

**{**

Pcell check total HARQ AN bit(vtdai),If the last occasion scheduled by SCELL has vtDai larger than current vtDai saved on P(S)Cell (on the same PUCCH resource), DL shall update vtDai to the largest one a from SCell, then DL shall update vtDai to UL.

**}**

**if** actK1OptForDPA(it is true,5G\_L2\_3076\_replaced([11141553](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23pHvvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled:\*\*\*\*

**{**

***\*In case: After Pcell DL scheduling done after step 2.7:***\*

Pcell DL scheduler should get max vtdai **based on DPA allocation for same PUCCH resource, sent to UL**.\*\*\*\*

**Pcell DL scheduler should send all DPA UEs's max vTdai to UL(even there is no DL scheduling for this UE)**, which will be used by UL scheduling(refer to **5G\_UP\_ALG\_5143\_replaced([11204128](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwjb8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**\*\*\*\*

***\*In case: After Pcell received Scell DL scheduling result after step 1.7:***\*

Pcell update A/N bit for Scell;

No need to update A/N bits change to UL.

**}**

[Before CNI-136896-A]

}

[End CNI-136896-A]

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11197235`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)

### (3)  P(S)Cell forwards HARQ feedback received either on PUCCH or PUSCH to remote SCell

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11197246`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
P(S)Cell L2-PS needs expected number of HARQ AN bits for local and remote SCells, saved in PUCCH bookkeeping table, to send the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq or UlData\_PuschReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL.

On reception of UlData\_PucchReceiveResp or UlData\_PuschReceiveResp, HARQ feedback related to remote SCell is not taken into account by P(S)Cell L2-PS in BLER computations (LA and Nack flood algorithms are carrier based) but are forwarded to the remote SCell L2-PS in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuXchReceiveIndHarqD. HARQ feedback bits from other carriers are filtered out so that SCell can process the HARQ feedback only with its own bookkeping table.

Note: In case a PUCCH F1 is scheduled for a UE on a slot matching with periodic SR, PCell 5G-L2-PS requests a double PUCCH F1 decoding (periodic F1 for SR plus the one signaled in the DCI) to 5G-L1-UL. Based on DTX information (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4615\_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PCell 5G-L2-PS selects the decoding results for actually transmitted PUCCH and forwards it to the SCell.

[Before CB006137-AC] In case P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS detects a GNB-UE misalignment on DRX cycles on reception of a PUCCH with DTX, an alignment command will be sent at beginning of next DL slot as part of 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_460. Refer to dedicated diagram in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_479 for more information on DRX notifications sent to SCell. [CB006137-AC] Refer to dedicated diagram in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1776 for more information on DRX notifications sent to SCell [End CB006137-AC]

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11197251`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)

### (4)  P(S)Cell forwards SCell CSI report to remote SCell

---

**8.2.2.2.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11197257`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
Note: If UCI field decoded by 5G-L1-UL also contains a periodic CSI report, this one is forwarded to corresponding peer L2-PS independently from current procedure (refer to MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_345).

---

#### 8.2.2.2.0-3 DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA) Error cases: (ID: 11197264)

**8.2.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11197270`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)

### Exc(1) DL HARQ Tx in SCell

---

**8.2.2.2.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11197275`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
Exc(1.7) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingInd

---

**8.2.2.2.0-3.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11197280`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
In case of PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingInd message loss, same defence as UlData\_PucchReceiveResp loss applies in SCell (too old HARQ are released).

However, DAI value sent by PCell 5G-L2-PS in DCI may not be consistent with SCell ones. PCell 5G-L2-PS may read invalid HARQ feedback value at erroneous bit position and trigger retransmissions at RLC level.

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating DRX (Discontinuous Reception) notifications between a primary cell (Pcell) and a secondary cell (Scell) in a mobile communication system. The diagram is divided into sections representing different scenarios and timeframes.
**Overall Structure:**
The diagram is organized horizontally by time slots, indicated by labels like N-3, N-2, N-1, N, M+1, M+2, M+3, M+4, and M+5. Vertically, it's divided into different communication paths and cell types:
\* **UL Airtime (+L1):** Represents uplink airtime.
\* **FDD (PCell):** Focuses on the PCell in Frequency Division Duplex mode.
\* **DL 5G-L2-PS:** Downlink data path for the PCell.
\* **UL 5G-L2-PS:** Uplink data path for the PCell.
\* **TDD (SCell):** Focuses on the SCell in Time Division Duplex mode.
\* **DL 5G-L2-PS:** Downlink data path for the SCell.
**Key Elements and Textual Information:**
\* **Title:** "DRX notifications betwenn P(S)cell and SCell"
\* **Top Bar:** "slot with HARQ feedback on PUCCH or PUSCH" and "L1 decoding" with an arrow indicating direction.
\* **UL Airtime (+L1) Bar:** Divided into segments labeled "N-3", "N-2", and "N-1".
\* **P(S)Cell -> Scell DRX notification:** A box indicating a notification from P(S)Cell to Scell.
\* **FDD (PCell) Section:**
\* **DL 5G-L2-PS Bar:** Divided into segments labeled "N-1" and "N".
\* **SCell -> P(S)cell DRX notification:** A box indicating a notification from Scell to P(S)cell.
\* **Blue Box (PCell Timers):** Contains "Pcell DL inactivity timer", "Pcell UL isInactivityTimerOn" (with a checkmark), and "Scell DL inactivity timer".
\* **Arrows and Events:**
\* An arrow from "Either UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD(N-3) Or UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD(N-3)" points to the "N-1" segment of the DL 5G-L2-PS bar.
\* A blue circle labeled "2" with text "rollback in case of DTX" points to the "N-1" segment.
\* A red circle labeled "3" with text "DL inactivity timer expiry" points to the "N" segment.
\* A yellow circle labeled "1" with text "UlToDlIntraSchedUpdate" and "> isInactivityTimerOn(UL)" points to the "N-1" segment.
\* "Pre-scheduling" is indicated with a double-headed arrow between "N-1" and "N" segments.
\* "PsPeerCtrl\_PcellStatusInd" with sub-items "> IsInactivityTimerOn", "= isInactivityTimerOn(UL) || isInactivityTimerOn(DL)", and "(reported when changed to False or HARQ feedback received)" points to the "N" segment.
\* **UL 5G-L2-PS Bar:** Divided into segments labeled "N-1" and "N".
\* **PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingInd:** A box with sub-items "> slot\_num", "> isNewTx", and "> isSentDuringDrxOn" is positioned above the UL 5G-L2-PS bar.
\* **TDD (SCell) Section:**
\* **DL 5G-L2-PS Bar:** Divided into segments labeled "M+1", "M+2", "M+3", "M+4", and "M+5".
\* **Blue Box (SCell Timers):** Contains "Pcell UL or DL isInactivityTimerOn" (with a checkmark) and "Scell DL inactivity timer".
\* **PsPeerCtrl\_ScellPuXchReceiveIndHarqD(N-3):** An arrow points from this text to the "M+5" segment of the DL 5G-L2-PS bar.
**Visual Representation:**
\* **Color Coding:** Different colored bars represent different states or types of data transmission. Yellow bars often indicate a specific timeframe or state (e.g., N-1, N-2), red bars might indicate an expiry or critical event, green bars might indicate a successful state, and blue/orange bars represent further time segments.
\* **Arrows:** Arrows are used extensively to show the flow of notifications, events, and data.
\* **Circles:** Numbered circles (1, 2, 3) highlight specific events or conditions.
\* **Checkmarks:** A checkmark next to "Pcell UL isInactivityTimerOn" and "Pcell UL or DL isInactivityTimerOn" suggests these timers are active or enabled.
\* **Clock Icons:** Clock icons next to timer names indicate they are related to inactivity timers.
\* **Dashed Lines:** Dashed lines separate different sections or modes (e.g., FDD PCell from TDD SCell).
The diagram visually depicts the complex interplay of DRX mechanisms, inactivity timers, and HARQ feedback in managing radio resources for both primary and secondary cells in different duplex modes.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2790.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB006137-AC]

For FR1 CA, each serving cell shall maintain its local DRX inactivityTimer. Each serving cell only use its own grant and HARQ feedback information to update the local DRX inactivityTimer state. Details refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15848\_replaced([11114393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpkDL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2267\_replaced([11114433](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpkqNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2274\_replaced([11114532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kplRS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Besides, each serving cell should maintain remote DRX inactivityTimer state. Remote DRX inactivityTimer update flow refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1776.

[End CB006137-AC]

**8.2.2.2.0-4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11197327`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
[Before CB006137-AC]

PsPeerCtrl\_SCellUeScheduleInd: only fresh SCell PDSCH transmissions during DRX on phases are used to start "SCell DL inactivity timer" in PCell to avoid cyclic rollback.

### [CB006137-AC]

**8.2.2.2.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11197333`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
Description of P(S)Cell to SCell DRX notification:

---

**8.2.2.2.0-4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11197343`)

DL HARQ Tx (inter-L2-PS DL CA)
[Before CB006137-AC]

(1) Reception of PsInternal\_UlToDlIntraSchedUpdate:

Indicates whether Pcell UL 5G-L2-PS has started or stopped its inactivity timer to update the UL DRX status flag in PCell DL.

(2) Reception of UlData\_PucchReceiveResp (or UlData\_PuschReceiveResp):

Manage PCell and SCell DL inactivity timers according to respective HARQ feedback:

- Ack/Nack proves that UE has received the Pcell or SCell PDCCH grant.

- DTX triggers a roll back (adjustement of inactivity timer according to last proved grant for this cell).

### Note that (2) may be received before (1).

(3) After checking DL inactivity timer expiry, PCell 5G-L2-PS sends a PsPeerCtrl\_PCellStatusInd to the SCell 5G-L2-PS to update the DRX status flag :

isInactivityTimerOn indicates if an inactivity timer is running in PCell (either in UL or DL).

This UE flag is only present in drxStateList when receiving a SCell HARQ feedback (2) or when it has changed to False because SCell must be synchronized as soon as possible.

### Please refer to 5G\_L2\_523\_replaced([11156434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24_LkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more information on DRX management.

### [CB006137-AC]

### For FR1 CA, new DRX inactivityTimer update flow refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1776 and 5G\_L2\_523\_replaced([11156434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24_LkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

### [End CB006137-AC]

#### 8.2.2.3.0-2 Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA) Description: (ID: 11197399)

**8.2.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197405`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
(1) Scell measurement start

---

**8.2.2.3.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13337213`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
for each DPA measurement period as per 5G\_RAN\_UP\_39209, Scell calculate each actived CA UE's cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx

PsPeerCtrl\_ScellMeasurementRep is used when:

**case1:  if there is CA UE with Scell activated:**

Scell start CA UE's measurement after Scell is actived, and calculate avatecs1AttemptRatioServingCellx;

**case2: if there is CA UE added(even without Scell activated):**

Scell need calculate Scell's PDSCH/PDCCH load, and calculate average load as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2727\_replaced([11121281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**case3:  if there is CA UE activated in Scell and Scell is DSS cell** [CB007372-H] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false **[End CB007372-H] , if there is new DSS bitmap updated from CRM, scell needs to fill DSS information to PsPeerCtrl\_ScellMeasurementRep.**[CB007372-H] if there is CA UE activated in Scell and Scell is DSS enabled and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true the L2-PS shall mark all slots in the DSS pattern for DPA as available for scheduling as specified in [12728590: DSS pattern for DPA in case of asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jM2gknHeEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) **[End CB007372-H]*****\****\*

---

**8.2.2.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11197416`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
(2) Scell send measurement report to Pcell

---

**8.2.2.3.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11197427`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
Scell need construct each PsPeerCtrl\_ScellMeasurementRep per remote Pcell, with corresponded UEs.

Scell fill IEs for each case as per step (1).

Scell send PsPeerCtrl\_ScellMeasurementRep to each Pcell.

[CB008140-AC]  
If Scell needs to send reports for more UEs than a single message can carry, it shall send the reports in subsequent message(s) in one slot – according to the DPA timers (see 5G\_L2\_593\_replaced([11158186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KKpvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_595\_replaced([11158240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KKrvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and assuming margin for Xp link delay (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12814\_replaced([11121981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  
[End CB008140-AC]

Pcell received reported measurement report from Scells, Save report result.

After received all Scell's report for case1, Pcell start DPA algorithm as per 5G\_L2\_595\_replaced([11158240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KKrvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.2.2.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11197432`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
(3) Pcell send DPA result to Scell

---

**8.2.2.3.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11197444`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
After DPA algorithm Done, Pcell filter out Scell's allocation per UE, and construct message as per 5G\_L2\_IF\_2119\_replaced([10980042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VfmRfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), notify each remote Scell.

[CB008140-AC]  
According to the 5G\_UP\_590\_replaced([11351541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubvCofvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), each PsPeerCtrl\_PcellPucchPreAllocationInd contains DPA CA allocation information per UE for one slot from the Scell scheduler period. All PsPeerCtrl\_PcellPucchPreAllocationInd shall be sent in the subsequent message(s) in one slot – according to the DPA timers (see 5G\_L2\_593\_replaced([11158186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KKpvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_595\_replaced([11158240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KKrvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and assuming margin for Xp link delay (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12814\_replaced([11121981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  
[End CB008140-AC]

After Scell received DPA result, Scell will use DPA for Scell CA UE scheduling.

---

**8.2.2.3.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11197449`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
(4) Pcell send Max DAI (UL CA UE) to Scell

---

**8.2.2.3.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11197460`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
case1: After DPA algorithm Done, Pcell filter out Scell's allocation per UL CA UE, and construct message PsPeerCtrl\_PcellDpaMaxDaiInd as per 5G\_L2\_IF\_2210\_replaced([10980081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VfmS_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), notify each remote UL CA Scell.

case2: When activing the Scell with UL CA configured, Pcell should use the message PsPeerCtrl\_PcellDpaMaxDaiInd to send the Max DAI of the activing UL CA UE to the Scell.

Note: If no DPA resource is not allocated for the UL CA UE, the Max DAI need not be sent to Scell.

After Scell received Max DAI, Scell will use Max DAI during Scell CA UE UL Pusch scheduling.

[CB009169-AB] Note: it's not applied to FR1 TDD + FDD UL CA refer to 5G\_L2\_7108\_replaced([11160809](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25W-_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  [End CB009169-AB]

---

#### 8.2.2.3.0-3 Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA) Error cases: (ID: 11197466)

**8.2.2.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11197473`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
Exc(2): PsPeerCtrl\_ScellMeasurementRep

---

**8.2.2.3.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11197477`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
if there is no latest measurement report from Scell, Pcell will use last report for DPA algorithm;

---

**8.2.2.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11197482`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
Exc(3): Pcell send DPA result to Scell

---

**8.2.2.3.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197487`)

Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA)
If there is message lost, Scell CA UE will have no PUCCH for one scheduler period;

if there is message delay, Scell CA UE will have no PUCCH for delayed slot untill DPA result is received.

---

Under "PCell-L2RT":
- "PCell 5G-L2-PS"
- "PCell 5G-L2-LO"
Under "SCell-L2RT":
- "SCell 5G-L2-PS"
- "SCell 5G-L2-LO"
Vertical lines represent the lifelines of these components. Arrows indicate messages being sent between them, along with labels describing the timing and the message content.
Specifically, the following interactions are shown:
1. An arrow originating from "PCell 5G-L2-LO" and pointing to "PCell 5G-L2-PS" is labeled "Every rdPeriodDIUserBufferMessage TTI" and "(20) PsPeerCtrl\_DIScellUeBufferStatusInd". This suggests a periodic message related to user buffer status is sent from LO to PS within the PCell.
2. An arrow originating from "SCell 5G-L2-PS" and pointing to "SCell 5G-L2-LO" is labeled "Every TTI" and "(10) LoCtrl\_DIBufferStatusInd". This indicates a message related to buffer status is sent every TTI (Transmission Time Interval) from PS to LO within the SCell.

#### 8.2.2.4.0-2 DL SCell UE buffer status update Description: (ID: 11197511)

**8.2.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197515`)

DL SCell UE buffer status update
(10) LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd

Direction: SCell 5G-L2-LO -> SCell 5G-L2-PS

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_870\_replaced([10984615](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBxwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.2.4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11197522`)

DL SCell UE buffer status update
5G-L2-LO bundles the DL Buffer Status Reports of several UEs and send them once per TTI. 5G-L2-PS after receiving the message stores the data in local storage.

---

**8.2.2.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11197526`)

DL SCell UE buffer status update
(20) PsPeerCtrl\_DlScellUeBufferStatusInd

Direction: SCell 5G-L2-PS -> PCell 5G-L2-PS

Message definition 5G\_L2\_IF\_2956\_replaced([10981071](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VniGPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.2.4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197532`)

DL SCell UE buffer status update
SCell 5G-L2-PS periodically, every rdPeriodDlUserBufferMessage TTI, sends the message towards PCell 5G-L2-PS with DL UE buffer statuses from local storage.

[CB015504-C]

MSC: Multi-L2RT CA

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "Start Flow Control on Scell" process within a Multi-L2RT CA (Carrier Aggregation) system. The diagram depicts interactions between different components: Primary\_L2RT, Secondary\_L2RT, and gNB\_DU.
The diagram is structured with lifelines representing these components, and messages exchanged between them are shown as arrows. The primary focus is on the flow control mechanisms initiated by the L2-LO (Layer 2 - Lower Layer) entity.
Here's a breakdown of the key elements and interactions:
**Components:**
\* **Primary\_L2RT:** Represents the primary radio link control entity.
\* **5G-Pcell-L2PS:** Primary Cell Layer 2 Packet Service.
\* **5G-Pcell-L2LO:** Primary Cell Layer 2 Lower Layer.
\* **Secondary\_L2RT:** Represents the secondary radio link control entity.
\* **5G-Scell-L2PS:** Secondary Cell Layer 2 Packet Service.
\* **5G-Scell-L2LO:** Secondary Cell Layer 2 Lower Layer.
\* **gNB\_DU:** Represents the base station's distributed unit.
\* **5G-L2-HI DU:** Layer 2 High Layer DU.
\* **5G-CP-RT:** Control Plane Real-Time.
**Key Interactions and Messages:**
1. **Start DL data flow on Scell:**
\* **(1) LoCtrl\_StartFlowControlReq:** A control message from the Primary\_L2RT (specifically from 5G-Pcell-L2LO) to the Secondary\_L2RT (5G-Scell-L2LO) to initiate flow control on the secondary cell. This message carries the interface identifier `5G_L2_IF_894`.
2. **L2-LO activates the Scell leg:** This is a descriptive text indicating the activation of the secondary cell's lower layer.
3. **LOOP on each non-GBR UE bearer in CA with Scell (possibly more than one in buffer-based activation):** This indicates a loop that processes each non-Guaranteed Bit Rate (non-GBR) User Equipment (UE) bearer within the Carrier Aggregation context, specifically for the secondary cell, and where buffer-based activation is possible.
4. **UE Data Delivery Status:**
\* **(2) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd:** A data indication message from the Secondary\_L2RT (5G-Scell-L2LO) to the Primary\_L2RT (5G-Pcell-L2LO). It signals the UE data delivery status, with `12LoActivatedForData=True`. The interface identifier is `5G_L2_IF_951`.
\* **primaryL2Lo.I2LoAvailableForDataSending = True** and **secondaryL2Lo.12LoAvailableForDataSending = True:** These are parameters within the status indication, confirming the availability of data sending for both primary and secondary L2LO entities.
5. **Data Transmission and Buffer Status:**
\* **(3) LoData\_DIRIcPduSendReq:** A data request message from the Secondary\_L2RT (5G-Scell-L2LO) to the Primary\_L2RT (5G-Pcell-L2LO) to send a Protocol Data Unit (PDU) along with its SDU buffer level. The interface identifier is `5G_L2_IF_933`. This message is shown to be sent before a specific event `CB015504-C`.
\* **(3) LoData\_DIDrbRIcPduSendReq:** Similar to the above, but specifically for Data Radio Bearer (DRB) PDUs.
\* **(4) LoCtrl\_DIBufferStatusInd:** A control indication message from the Primary\_L2RT (5G-Pcell-L2LO) to the Secondary\_L2RT (5G-Scell-L2LO) reporting the buffer status at the L2LO buffer level and SDU buffer level. The interface identifier is `5G_L2_IF_874`.
6. **New traffic in Scell (new PDUs):** This is a descriptive text indicating the arrival of new traffic data.
7. **Data split mode in L2-HI:** This is a descriptive text indicating that data is being split in the L2-HI (Layer 2 High Layer) component.
8. **Traffic goes on in Pcell including new PDUs:** This indicates that traffic is now being handled by the primary cell, including the newly arrived PDUs.
9. **Further Data Transmission and Buffer Status:**
\* **(5) LoData\_DIRIcPduSendReq:** Another data request message for PDUs, sent before `CB015504-C`.
\* **(5) Alt:** Indicates an alternative path or condition.
\* **(5A.1) If SRB RLC PDU:** A conditional message related to Signaling Radio Bearer (SRB) RLC PDUs.
\* **(5A2) LoData\_DISrbRIcPduSendReq:** Data request for SRB PDUs.
\* **(5B.1) If DRB RLC PDU:** A conditional message related to Data Radio Bearer (DRB) RLC PDUs.
\* **(5B) LoData\_DIDrbRIcPduSendReq:** Data request for DRB PDUs.
\* **(6) LoCtrl\_DIBufferStatusInd:** Another buffer status indication message from Primary\_L2RT to Secondary\_L2RT.
10. **On-going and/or remaining traffic in Pcell:** Descriptive text indicating the handling of ongoing or remaining traffic in the primary cell.
11. **More UE Data Delivery Status:**
\* **(7) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd:** Similar to message (2), indicating UE data delivery status with `12LoActivatedForData=NoChange`. Interface `5G_L2_IF_951`.
\* **(8) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd:** Another UE data delivery status indication, also with `12LoActivatedForData=NoChange`. Interface `5G_L2_IF_951`.
12. **Final Data Transmission:**
\* **(9) LoData\_DIRIcPduSendReq:** Data request for PDUs, sent before `CB015504-C`.
\* **(9) LoData\_DIDrbRIcPduSendReq:** Data request for DRB PDUs.
The diagram visually represents the control flow and data path management when initiating flow control on a secondary cell in a multi-L2RT CA scenario, highlighting the roles of different L2 entities and the exchange of control and data messages. The use of colored backgrounds (yellow and light green) helps to delineate different phases or contexts of the interaction.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/12819201\_Start Flow Control on SCell.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[End CB015504-C]

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11197584`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
UE-level message (5G\_L2\_IF\_887\_replaced([10984843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WC_6vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from secondary L2-PS to secondary L2-LO on first remote Scell activation **or Scell resume after deactivation** [CB013709-CB] or overload goes down so active SCell requires DL data transmission again as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31954\_replaced([11122234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), **[End CB013709-CB]**\*\*\*\*

L2-LO is requested to activate the secondary path for all DRBs that can be scheduled on this path

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
(2) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd (l2LoActivatedForData=True,...)

---

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197594`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
Secondary L2-LO starts DL flow control on secondary path for each DRB that can be scheduled on the path (stated in Bearer setup or Bearer modify in L2-HI (DU))

Secondary L2-LO sets l2LoActivatedForData=True (5G\_L2\_IF\_2375\_replaced([10986071](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WMw4Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to switch-on DL traffic from L2-HI (DU) on the secondary path

L2-HI switches internal state secondaryL2LO.l2LoAvailableForDataSending to True for the bearer

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
**(5) LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (up to 26R1)**

---

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11197625`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
Case of "data split mode" in L2-HI (DU) (RLC sends "new" DL PDUs on both primary and secondary path, from internal L2-HI (DU) settings)

Both "new" and remaining DL PDUs in the primary L2-LO DL buffer (not flushed) are scheduled on primary path

Primary L2-LO sends LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd to primary L2-PS as a request for scheduling DL DPUs in the primary L2-LO buffer

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
(5) Optional

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `12819569`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
In case of "data split mode" in L2-HI (DU):

RLC sends "new" DL PDUs on both primary (SRB/DRB RLC PDUs) and secondary (DRB PDUs only) path, from internal L2-HI (DU) settings

Both "new" and remaining DL PDUs in the primary L2-LO DL buffer (not flushed) are scheduled on primary path

Primary L2-LO sends LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd to primary L2-PS as a request for scheduling DL DPUs in the primary L2-LO buffer

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11197649`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
Primary L2-LO sends LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd for traffic on primary path

Primary L2-LO sets l2LoActivatedForData=NoChange since the primary path state is not changed (still active/True) from L2-LO pov

---

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-13**  (ID: `11197654`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
(8) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd (l2LoActivatedForData=NoChange,...)

---

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11197660`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
Secondary L2-LO sends LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd for traffic on secondary path

Secondary L2-LO sets l2LoActivatedForData=NoChange since the secondary path state is not changed (active/True) from L2-LO pov

---

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-14**  (ID: `11197666`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
**(9) LoData\_DlRlcPduSendReq (up to 26R1)**

---

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11197671`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
L2-HI (DU) goes on sending "new" RLC DL PDU of the bearer to secondary L2-LO [5GC001390-FA] or also to primary L2-LO [End 5GC001390-FA]

---

**8.2.3.1.0-2.0-15**  (ID: `12819422`)

DL Data Transfer start on secondary path
**(9) LoData\_DlDrbRlcPduSendReq**

Direction: 5G-L2-HI(DU) -> 5G-L2-LO

Message definition: [12805904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_CSqZtZ-MEfCkxIKMlo4L6w)

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating "DL Data Transfer Stop during SCell release transient phase (Multi L2-RT CA)".
The diagram depicts interactions between different components: "Primary L2-RT", "gNB-DU", and "Secondary L2-RT". Within these components, specific entities are shown: "5G-Pcell-L2PS", "5G-Pcell-L2LO", "5G-Scell-L2PS", "5G-Scell-L2LO", and "5G-L2-HI DU".
The main flow of the diagram is within the "gNB-DU" and "Secondary L2-RT" sections, focusing on "Secondary path deactivation".
The sequence of events is as follows:
1. **1: LoCtrl\_StopFlowControlReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_902)**: A request is sent from "5G-Scell-L2PS" to "5G-Scell-L2LO".
2. **Loop (for each DRB)**: This indicates a process that iterates for each Data Radio Bearer (DRB).
\* **2: LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_951)**: An indication is sent from "5G-Scell-L2LO" to "5G-L2-HI DU".
\* **3: message dropped (secondary DL path already deconfigured)**: This is a state or event occurring within the loop, indicating that messages are dropped because the secondary DL path is already deconfigured.
3. **4: Flush L2-LO buffer**: This action is performed by "5G-Scell-L2LO".
The diagram also includes a URL at the bottom: "https://gitlab.com/msc-generator v8.2".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2870.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

#### 8.2.3.3.0-2 DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase Description: (ID: 11197777)

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197780`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
(1a) LoCtrl\_StopFlowControlReq

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11197792`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
UE-level message from Secondary L2-PS to Secondary L2-LO to stop DL traffic for all bearers of the UE mapped on the secondary path**.**

**[CB013709-CB] One of its trigger condition is: when SCell DL scheduler RT load goes up and requires no more DL data according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31954\_replaced([11122234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** [End CB013709-CB]\*\*\*\*

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11197796`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
(1b) HARQ buffer indexes release & DL buffer level reset

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197801`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
For this UE, the Secondary L2-PS

* releases the dlHarqBufferIndex for each still pending DL HARQ retransmission process
* resets the level of DL buffer data associated to this UE.

No data will be scheduled any more by the Secondary L2-PS for this UE.

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11197807`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
(2) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd (l2LoActivatedForData=False,...)

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11197812`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
The Secondary L2-LO stops the DL flow control on the secondary DL path for each UE DRB of the Secondary L2-RT.

The SCell L2-LO sends a last DDDS flow control message (with indication l2LoActivatedForData=False) for each UE DRB.

Note: at this stage, the secondary DL path is already deconfigured in L2-HI, therefore the last DDDS flow control message sent for each UE DRB will be ignored by L2-HI.

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11197819`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
(3) Message drop

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11197825`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
At this stage the Secondary DL path is already deconfigured. Therefore, any received DDDS flow control message is ignored.

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11197832`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
(4) Flush of the L2-LO buffer

---

**8.2.3.3.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11197838`)

DL Data Transfer stop during SCell release transient phase
SCell L2-LO flushes each UE bearer DL RLC PDU buffer.

---

Multi-L2RT CA (see also 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_529)
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a "Multi-L2RT CA Stop Flow Control on Scell" scenario. The diagram depicts interactions between different network functions, including Primary\_L2RT, Secondary\_L2RT, gNB\_DU, 5G-Pcell-L2PS, 5G-Pcell-L2LO, 5G-Scell-L2PS, 5G-Scell-L2LO, 5G-L2-HI DU, and 5G-CP-RT.
The diagram shows the following sequence of events:
1. **DL data flow stopped on Scell**: This is a condition or event that triggers the subsequent actions.
2. **(1) LoCtrl\_StopFlowControlReq 5G\_L2\_IF\_902**: A request is sent from 5G-Scell-L2PS to 5G-Scell-L2LO to stop the flow control.
3. **No HARQ buffer flush (discarded on next use)**: A dotted arrow indicates that there is no HARQ buffer flush, and it will be discarded on next use. This message is sent from 5G-Scell-L2LO to 5G-L2-HI DU.
4. **Flush RLC PDU**: A message is sent from 5G-Scell-L2LO to 5G-Scell-L2PS to flush RLC PDU.
5. **LOOP on each bearer that was scheduled on Scell**: This indicates a loop that iterates through each bearer scheduled on Scell.
6. **(2) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd (I2LoActivatedForData=False) 5G\_L2\_IF\_951**: An indication is sent from 5G-Scell-L2LO to 5G-Scell-L2PS regarding the UE data delivery status, with `I2LoActivatedForData` set to `False`.
7. Inside the loop, the following conditions are checked and actions are taken:
\* **secondaryL2Lo.I2LoAvailableForDataSending = False**
\* **primaryL2Lo.I2LoAvailableForDataSending = True**
8. **Traffic switched to Poell**: This indicates that traffic is switched to Poell.
9. **no DL PDU sent to Scell**: This indicates that no Downlink PDUs are sent to Scell.
10. **Reset L2-LO buffer status Stop pending HARQ retrans processes**: These are actions performed by 5G-Scell-L2LO.
The diagram also includes a URL at the bottom right: `https://gitlab.com/msc-generator v8.2`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2885.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
 
 
 
 
save at :

---

#### 8.2.3.4.0-2 DL Data Transfer Stop in secondary path in intra-gNB CA Description: (ID: 11197864)

**8.2.3.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197870`)

DL Data Transfer Stop in secondary path in intra-gNB CA
(1) LoCtrl\_StopFlowControlReq

---

**8.2.3.4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11197875`)

DL Data Transfer Stop in secondary path in intra-gNB CA
UE-level message from Secondary L2-PS to Secondary L2-LO to stop DL traffic for all bearers of the UE on secondary path.

Secondary L2-LO flushes each bearer DL RLC PDU buffer.

Secondary L2-PS releases all its dlHarqBufferIndex related to the still pending DL HARQ retransmission process for this UE.

Note : For dlHarqBufferIndex management refer to 5G\_L2\_1976\_replaced([11217544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_ElavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In addition Secondary L2-PS resets its DL buffer data level for this UE.

No data will be scheduled any more by Secondary L2-PS for this UE.

---

**8.2.3.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11197880`)

DL Data Transfer Stop in secondary path in intra-gNB CA
(2) LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd (l2LoActivatedForData=False,...)

---

**8.2.3.4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11197886`)

DL Data Transfer Stop in secondary path in intra-gNB CA
Secondary L2-LO stops DL flow control on secondary path for each DRB that can be scheduled on the path

Secondary L2-LO sets l2LoActivatedForData=False to switch-off DL traffic from L2-HI (DU) on the secondary path

L2-HI switches internal state secondaryL2LO.l2LoAvailableForDataSending to False for the bearer

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "DL Data Transfer Stop" procedure.
The diagram depicts interactions between different components: "prime-gNB (5G-L2-HI PCell)", "ext-gNB (5G-L2-LO ext-SCell)", and "ext-gNB (5G-L2-PS ext-SCell)". A "Timer" is also shown as a component within the "ext-gNB".
The procedure is divided into "Outer procedures" which contain optional ("Opt") and looped ("Loop") sections.
The sequence of events is as follows:
1. **(1) Is Stop flow control required?**: This is a question posed by the "ext-gNB (5G-L2-LO ext-SCell)" to itself or another internal component.
2. **(2) LoCtrl\_StopFlowControlReq**: A request message is sent from "ext-gNB (5G-L2-LO ext-SCell)" to "ext-gNB (5G-L2-PS ext-SCell)".
3. **(3) Update scheduling weights and stop scheduling**: This action is performed by "ext-gNB (5G-L2-PS ext-SCell)".
4. **(4) For each DRB**: This indicates a loop that iterates over each Dedicated Radio Bearer (DRB).
5. **(5) (GTP-U) DU DL Data Delivery Status (Scell Activation Status = False)**: Within the loop, a status update is sent, indicating that the Secondary Cell (Scell) activation status is False. This message is sent from "ext-gNB (5G-L2-PS ext-SCell)" to "prime-gNB (5G-L2-HI PCell)".
The diagram also includes a reference label "Ref" and a footer with a URL: "https://gitlab.com/msc-generator v7.3.1".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2894.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "Inter-gNB CA Bearer Stop in ext-gNB" procedure.
The diagram is divided into two main participants: "prime-gNB" and "ext-gNB". Each participant is further subdivided into functional blocks.
Under "prime-gNB", there are three blocks: "5G-L2-PS PCell", "5G-L2-HI PCell", and "5G-CP-RT".
Under "ext-gNB", there are four blocks: "5G-L2-LO ext-SCell", "5G-L2-PS ext-SCell", and "Timer".
The diagram depicts a sequence of messages and actions:
1. **Ref**: "Outer procedure: DRB deletion for CA (SA)" is indicated as a reference point.
2. **Message (1)**: A message labeled "(1) PsUser\_BearerStopReq (ext-SCell and DRB lists)" is sent from the "prime-gNB" (specifically from the "5G-L2-HI PCell" or "5G-CP-RT" to the "5G-L2-PS PCell" or vice versa, indicated by the arrow originating from the left and pointing to the right, spanning across the prime-gNB section).
3. **Loop**: A loop construct is shown, labeled "(2) For each ext-SCell". This indicates that the subsequent steps will be repeated for each secondary cell (ext-SCell).
4. **Message (3)**: Within the loop, a message labeled "(3) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellDrbStopReq (DRB list)" is sent from the "prime-gNB" (specifically from the "5G-L2-HI PCell" or "5G-CP-RT") to the "ext-gNB" (specifically to the "5G-L2-LO ext-SCell" or "5G-L2-PS ext-SCell"). The arrow indicates a communication to the right.
5. **Action (4)**: A shaded oval represents an action labeled "(4) DL Data Transfer Stop". This action occurs within the "ext-gNB" participant, likely triggered by the previous message.
6. **Ref**: Another reference point, "DRB deletion for CA (SA) continues", is shown at the bottom.
7. **URL**: A URL "https://gitlab.com/msc-generator v7.3.1" is present at the bottom right corner.
The overall diagram illustrates the process of stopping bearers in a Carrier Aggregation (CA) scenario between a primary gNB and an external gNB, specifically focusing on the deletion of Data Radio Bearers (DRBs).[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2910.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "MSC575 Single carrier PDCP average downlink throughput". The diagram depicts interactions between four entities: 5G-L2-HI DU, 5G-L2-HI CU, 5GC, and CP-NRT.
The diagram shows a series of messages exchanged between these entities, numbered from (1) to (14). These messages represent various events and data transfers, such as PDCP SDUs and PDCP PDUs, timer start and expiry events, and F1-U DDDS (DDR) messages. There is also a dashed box labeled "Burst Time Report" indicating a potential reporting mechanism.
The sequence of events is as follows:
- (1) PDCP SDU n is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
- (2) Guard timer n starts on 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (3) PDCP PDU n is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (4) PDCP SDU n+1 is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
- (5) Guard timer n+1 starts on 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (6) PDCP PDU n+1 is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (7) Guard timer n expires on 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (8) F1-U DDDS (DDR) is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
- A note indicates "more PDUs within burst".
- (9) PDCP SDU m is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
- (10) Guard timer m starts on 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (11) PDCP PDU m is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (12) Guard timer m-1 expires on 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (13) Guard timer m expires on 5G-L2-HI CU.
- (14) Alt indicates an alternative scenario.
- Within the alternative scenario, F1-U DDDS (DDR) is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
- PDCP SDU is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
- HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq is sent from 5GC to CP-NRT.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2929.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

The diagram shows a series of messages exchanged between these components, numbered from (1) to (15). These messages represent PDCP SDUs and PDUs, guard timers, retention delay timers, and F1-U DDDS (DDR) requests.
Specifically, the diagram shows:
- PDCP SDU n being sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC, triggering a retention delay timer start.
- Guard timer n starting and expiring.
- PDCP SDU n+1 being sent, followed by PDCP PDU n+1.
- Guard timer n+1 starting and the retention delay timer expiring.
- An F1-U DDDS (DDR) message being sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
- A section indicating "more PDUs within burst".
- PDCP SDU m being sent, followed by PDCP PDU m.
- Guard timer m starting, and guard timers m-1 and m expiring.
- An alternative flow (15) Alt, which also involves F1-U DDDS (DDR), PDCP SDU, and a HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq message.
The diagram uses solid arrows for message transmission and dashed arrows for timer events. A dashed box labeled "Burst Time Report" is also present, indicating a potential reporting mechanism.
