[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "MSC575 Single carrier PDCP average downlink throughput". The diagram depicts interactions between four entities: 5G-L2-HI DU, 5G-L2-HI CU, 5GC, and CP-NRT.
The diagram shows a series of messages exchanged between these entities, numbered from (1) to (13).
Here's a breakdown of the interactions:
\* **Initial State/Condition:** A hexagonal box labeled "[CB008225-B-UPD003]" indicates a condition where "Either bearer is in Active state OR Bearer transitions from Inactive to Active state". This condition is followed by "[End CB008225-B-UPD003]".
\* **Message Flow:**
\* (1) PDCP SDU n is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
\* (2) PDCP PDU n is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* (3) "Retention Delay and Guard timer for PDCP PDU n start" is initiated by 5G-L2-HI CU, with a dashed arrow pointing to 5GC.
\* (4) PDCP SDU n+1 is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
\* (5) PDCP PDU n+1 is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* (6) "Guard timer recalculation for PDCP PDU n+1" is initiated by 5G-L2-HI CU, with a dashed arrow pointing to 5GC.
\* (7) "Retention delay timer expires" is indicated by a dashed arrow from 5GC to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* (8) F1-U DDDS is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* A note "more PDUs within burst" is present.
\* (9) PDCP SDU m is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
\* (10) PDCP PDU m is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* (11) "Guard timer recalculation for PDCP PDU m" is initiated by 5G-L2-HI CU, with a dashed arrow pointing to 5GC.
\* (12) "Guard timer expires" is indicated by a dashed arrow from 5GC to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* **Alternative Flow (13) Alt:** This section shows an alternative scenario.
\* F1-U DDDS is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* PDCP SDU is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
\* HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq is sent from 5GC to CP-NRT.
\* HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq is sent from 5GC to CP-NRT.
The diagram also includes a dashed box labeled "Burst Time Report" which appears to be a separate reporting mechanism.
The title of the diagram is "MSC575 Single carrier PDCP average downlink throughput".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_2934.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Description:
(2) Guard Timer n starts

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11198175`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start GT n with sending PDCP PDU n towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall not count GT n to ThpTimeDl (due to is Retention Delay).

---

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start observing the burst.

**8.2.4.1.2.0-1.0-14**  (ID: `11198303`)

Description:
(14) Alternative End of Burst

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-1.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11198308`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall detect end of burst after:

o GT m expiry on DDDS arrival OR

o GT m expiry on new PDU sent OR

o bearer delete

 For each case described above 5G-L2-Hi CU shall update

ThpVolDl according to the formula: ThpVolDl += PDCP PDU n + … + PDCP PDU m

and

ThpTimeDl according to the formula: GT m expiry - GT n expiry.

o bearer delete

 For each case described above 5G-L2-Hi CU shall update

ThpVolDl according to the formula: ThpVolDl += PDCP PDU n + … + PDCP PDU m

and

ThpTimeDl according to the formula: GT m expiry - GT n expiry.

---

##### 8.2.4.1.2.0-3 Description: Valid from 02647778 onwards (ID: 11198486)

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11198492`)

Description:
(1) PDCP SDU n

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11198502`)

Description:
5G-L2-Hi CU shall process PDCP SDU n into PDCP PDU n.

[CNI-112795]

5G-L2-Hi CU has PDCP PDU n to retransmit for intra-gNB HO with dataDuplication=TRUE.

[End CNI-112795]

5G-L2-Hi CU shall consider start of a new burst.

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11198507`)

Description:
(1.1) Conditions to proceed further with data transfer from 5G-L2-HI-CU to 5G-L2-HI-DU

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11198513`)

Description:
 Either the bearer should be in Active state when the PDCP SDU is received

 OR the bearer shall be transitioned to Active state from Inactive state, if the bearer was in Inactive state when the PDCP SDU was received.

NOTE : In case the bearer is not active OR the bearer will not become active, PDCP SDU is not sent to RLC.

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11198517`)

Description:
(2) PDCP PDU n

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11198527`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU n towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start GT for PDCP PDU n as per formula: (PDCP PDU n Volume/avgEstTput[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795].

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start Retention Delay timer as per: avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795].

where:

* avgEstTput[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795] and avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795] can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11198532`)

Description:
(3) Retention Delay Timer and Guard Timer for PDCP PDU n start

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11198536`)

Description:
 5G-L2-HI CU shall not count Retention Delay Time to ThpTimeDl.

 5G-L2-HI CU shall start Retention Delay timer and GT for PDCP PDU n with sending PDCP PDU n towards 5G-L2-HI DU.

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11198541`)

Description:
(4) PDCP SDU n+1

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11198553`)

Description:
 5G-L2-HI CU shall process PDCP SDU n+1 into PDCP PDU n+1.

 5G-L2-HI CU shall consider PDCP SDU n+1 to the same burst as PDCP SDU n [Before CNI-112795]due to gNB buffer is not empty and[CNI-112795] as there is at-least one PDCP SDU which is yet to be sent to 5G-L2-HI DU or [End CNI-112795] GT is running.

[CNI-112795]

 5G-L2-HI CU shall consider PDCP PDU n+1 to the same burst if this needs to be retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU for intra-gNB HO with dataDuplication=true.

[End CNI-112795]

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11198559`)

Description:
(5) PDCP PDU n+1

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11198571`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU n+1 towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall recalculate GT for PDCP PDU n+1 as per formula: (PDCP PDU n+1 Volume/avgEstTput[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795].

where:

* avgEstTput[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795] and avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795] can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `11198576`)

Description:
(6) Guard Timer recalculation for PDCP PDU n+1

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11198581`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall recalculate GT for PDCP PDU n+1 with sending PDCP PDU n+1 towards 5G-L2-Hi DU, compare with the running GT and choose the latest GT expiry time.

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-8**  (ID: `11198587`)

Description:
(7) Retention Delay Timer expires

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11198592`)

Description:
 At Retention Delay Timer expiry, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start counting the time of the burst for the report (thpTimeDl).

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-9**  (ID: `11198597`)

Description:
(8) Downlink Data Delivery Status

Direction: 5G-L2-HI DU -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5815\_replaced([11222283](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx6t4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11198609`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall evaluate if [Before PR794319][Before CNI-112795]buffer is empty or[End CNI-112795] there are SDUs still waiting for transmission [CNI-112795] or if there are PDCP PDUs still waiting for retransmission for intra-gNB HO with dataDuplication=true [End CNI-112795][PR794319] buffer is empty[End PR794319] within the burst.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall check if GT is running.

[CNI-112795] DDDS influences the GT calculation which depends on DBS and DataOnFlight.[End CNI-112795]

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-10**  (ID: `11198616`)

Description:
(9) PDCP SDU m

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `11198630`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall process PDCP SDU m into PDCP PDU m.

 5G-L2-HI CU shall consider PDCP SDU m to the same burst as PDCP SDU n and PDCP SDU n+1 [Before CNI-112795]due to gNB buffer is not empty and [CNI-112795] [Before PR794319]as there is at least one PDCP SDU which needs to be sent to 5G-L2-HI DU or[PR794319] as the gNB buffer is not empty and[End PR794319][End CNI-112795] GT is running.

[CNI-112795]

 5G-L2-HI CU shall consider PDCP PDU m to the same burst if this needs to be retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU for intra-gNB HO with dataDuplication=true.

[End CNI-112795]

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-11**  (ID: `11198636`)

(10) PDCP PDU m

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-11.0-2**  (ID: `11198649`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU m towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall recalculate GT for PDCP PDU m as per formula: (PDCP PDU m Volume/avgEstTput[Before CNI-112795] m[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] m[End CNI-112795].

where:

* avgEstTput[Before CNI-112795] m[End CNI-112795] and avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] m[End CNI-112795] can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11198663`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi shall recalculate GT for PDCP PDU m with sending of PDCP PDU m towards 5G-L2-Hi DU, compare with the running GT and choose the latest GT expiry time.

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-13**  (ID: `11198671`)

Description:
(12) Guard Timer expires

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-13.0-2**  (ID: `11198685`)

Description:
 At GT expiry, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall end counting the time of the burst for the report (thpTimeDl) due to [Before PR794319] there is no PDCP SDU waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-Hi DU [CNI-112795] or there is no PDCP PDU waiting for retransmission in intra-gNB HO scenario with dataDuplication=true[End CNI-112795][PR794319] the gNB buffer is empty.[End PR794319](that is considered as end of the burst).

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-14**  (ID: `11198692`)

Description:
(13) Alternative End of Burst

---

**8.2.4.1.2.0-3.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11198697`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall detect end of burst after:

o GT expiry on DDDS arrival OR

o GT expiry on new SDU receive OR

o bearer delete OR

o bearer modification with nrCellIdentity change

 For each case described above 5G-L2-Hi CU shall update

ThpVolDl according to the formula: ThpVolDl += PDCP SDU n + … + PDCP SDU m

and

ThpTimeDl according to the formula: GT expiry - Retention Delay timer expiry.

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "MSC1080 EN-DC PDCP average downlink throughput counter" process. The diagram depicts interactions between several network entities: LTE L2, 5G-L2-HI DU, 5G-L2-HI CU, 5GC, and CP-NRT.
The diagram shows a series of messages exchanged between these entities, indicated by arrows. The messages are numbered from 1 to 18, with a separate section labeled "(19) Alt" showing alternative scenarios.
Here's a breakdown of the interactions:
\* **Initial PDCP SDUs and Timers:** The process begins with PDCP SDU 'n' being sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC (1). The 5GC then starts a "Retention Delay timer" (2) and a "Guard timer n" (4). PDCP SDU 'n+1' is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC (5), triggering the start of "Guard timer n+1" (7). The "Retention delay timer" expires (8).
\* **F1-U DDDS and More PDUs:** The 5G-L2-HI DU sends an "F1-U DDDS (DDR)" message to 5G-L2-HI CU (9). Following this, "more PDUs within burst" are indicated, leading to PDCP SDU 'm-1' being sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC (10). This triggers "Guard timer m-1 starts" (12).
\* **Timer Expirations and PDCP SDUs:** "Guard timer n+1 expires" (13). PDCP SDU 'm' is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC (14), initiating "Guard timer m starts" (16). Subsequently, "Guard timer m-1 expires" (17) and "Guard timer m expires" (18).
\* **Alternative Scenarios (19 Alt):** This section shows alternative message flows:
\* An "X2-U DDDS (DDR)" message is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* An "F1-U DDDS (DDR)" message is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU.
\* A "PDCP SDU" message is sent from 5G-L2-HI CU to 5GC.
\* A "HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq" message is sent from 5GC to CP-NRT.

The diagram shows a sequence of messages exchanged between these entities, including PDCP SDUs, PDCP PDUs, and various timer-related messages like "Retention Delay timer" and "Guard timer". There are also messages related to bearer state transitions and DDDS (Data Discarding and Delivery Service).

A dashed box labeled "Burst Time Report" indicates a separate, possibly asynchronous, reporting mechanism. A section labeled "(18) Alt" shows an alternative flow involving X2-U DDDS, F1-U DDDS, PDCP SDU, HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq, and HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq.
The text within the diagram describes the messages and conditions of the sequence. Key elements include:
\* **Title:** MSC618 EN-DC PDCP average downlink throughput counter
\* **Lifelines:** LTE L2, 5G-L2-HI DU, 5G-L2-HI CU, 5GC, Burst Time Report, CP-NRT
\* **Messages:**
\* (1) PDCP SDUn
\* [CB008225-B-UPD003] (1.1) Either bearer is in Active state OR Bearer transitions from Inactive to Active state [End CB008225-B-UPD003]
\* (2) PDCP PDU n
\* (3) F1-U Retention Delay timer and Guard timer for PDCP PDU n start
\* (4) PDCP SDU n+1
\* (5) PDCP PDU n+1
\* (6) X2-U Retention Delay timer and Guard timer for PDCP PDU n+1 start
\* (7) F1-U Retention delay timer expires
\* (8) X2-U Retention delay timer expires
\* (9) F1-U DDDS
\* more PDUs within burst
\* (10) PDCP SDU m-1
\* (11) PDCP PDU m-1
\* (12) F1-U Guard timer recalculation for PDCP PDU m-1
\* (13) PDCP SDU m
\* (14) PDCP PDU m
\* (15) X2-U Guard timer recalculation for PDCP PDU m
\* (16) F1-U Guard timer expires
\* (17) X2-U Guard timer expires
\* **Alternative Flow (18) Alt:**
\* X2-U DDDS
\* F1-U DDDS
\* PDCP SDU
\* HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq
\* HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq
The diagram uses standard UML sequence diagram notation, with solid arrows representing synchronous messages and dashed arrows representing asynchronous messages or replies. **8.2.4.2.2.0-1.0-18**  (ID: `11199011`)

Description:
(18) Alternative End of Burst

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-1.0-18.0-1**  (ID: `11199017`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall detect end of burst after:

o GT m expiry on DDDS arrival OR

o GT m expiry on new PDU sent OR

o bearer delete

 For each case described above 5G-L2-Hi CU shall update

ThpVolDl according to the formula: ThpVolDl = LteThpVolDl + NrThpVolDl,

where: LteThpVolDl = (PDCP PDU n+1) + (PDCP PDU m)

NrThpVolDl = (PDCP PDU n) + (PDCP PDU m-1)

and

ThpTimeDl according to the formula: GT m expiry - GT n expiry.

---

NrThpVolDl = (PDCP PDU n) + (PDCP PDU m-1)

and

##### 8.2.4.2.2.0-3 Description: Valid from 02647778 onwards (ID: 11199294)

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11199300`)

Description:
(1) PDCP SDU n

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11199314`)

Description:
5G-L2-Hi CU shall process PDCP SDU n into PDCP PDU n.

[CNI-112795]

5G-L2-Hi CU has PDCP PDU n to retransmit for intra-gNB HO with dataDuplication=TRUE.

[End CNI-112795]

5G-L2-Hi CU shall consider start of a new burst.

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11199320`)

Description:
(1.1) Conditions to proceed further with data transfer from 5G-L2-HI-CU to 5G-L2-HI-DU

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11199327`)

Description:
 Either the bearer should be in Active state when the PDCP SDU is received

 OR the bearer shall be transitioned to Active state from Inactive state, if the bearer was in Inactive state when the PDCP SDU was received.

NOTE : In case the bearer is not active OR the bearer will not become active, PDCP SDU is not sent to RLC.

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11199333`)

Description:
(2) PDCP PDU n

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11199349`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU n towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start F1-U GT for PDCP PDU n as per formula: PDCP PDU n Volume/avgEstTput[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795].

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start F1-U Retention Delay timer as per: avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795].

where:

* avgEstTput[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795] and avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n[End CNI-112795] can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11199354`)

Description:
(3) F1-U Retention Delay Timer and Guard Timer for PDCP PDU n start

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11199361`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall not count F1-U Retention Delay Time to ThpTimeDl.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start F1-U Retention Delay timer and GT for PDCP PDU n with sending PDCP PDU n towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11199368`)

Description:
(4) PDCP SDU n+1

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11199380`)

Description:
 5G-L2-HI CU shall process PDCP SDU n+1 into PDCP PDU n+1.

 5G-L2-HI CU shall consider PDCP SDU n+1 to the same burst as PDCP SDU n [Before CNI-112795]due to gNB buffer is not empty and[CNI-112795] [Before PR794319]as there is at-least one PDCP SDU which is yet to be sent to 5G-L2-HI DU or[PR794319] as the gNB buffer is empty and [End PR794319] [End CNI-112795] GT is running.

[CNI-112795]

 5G-L2-HI CU shall consider PDCP PDU n+1 to the same burst if this needs to be retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU for intra-gNB HO with dataDuplication=true.

[End CNI-112795]

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11199386`)

Description:
(5) PDCP PDU n+1

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> LTE L2

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11199399`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU n+1 towards LTE L2 and start GT n+1.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start X2-U GT for PDCP PDU n+1 as per formula: (PDCP PDU n+1 Volume/avgEstTputX2[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelayX2[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795].

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start X2-U Retention Delay timer as per: avgPduDelvDelay[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795].

where:

* avgEstTputX2[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795] and avgPduDelvDelayX2[Before CNI-112795] n+1[End CNI-112795] can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start X2-U Retention Delay timer and GT for PDCP PDU n+1 with sending PDCP PDU n+1 towards LTE L2.

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-10**  (ID: `11199443`)

Direction: 5G-L2-HI DU -> 5G-L2-HI CU

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall evaluate if [before PR794319][Before CNI-112795]buffer is empty or [End CNI-112795] there are SDUs still waiting for transmission within the burst [CNI-112795] or if there are PDCP PDUs still waiting for retransmission within the burst for intra-gNB HO with dataDuplication=true [End CNI-112795][PR794319] the buffer if empty[End PR794319].

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall check if any GT is running.

[CNI-112795] DDDS influences the GT calculation which depends on DBS and DataOnFlight.[End CNI-112795]

Description:
(16) Last F1-U Guard Timer expires

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11199561`)

Description:
 5G-L2-HI CU shall not consider last F1-U GT expiry (due to X2-U GT is still running) and still continue counting the thpTimeDl. L2Hi shall choose the latest running GT timer to stop counting the time of the burst for the report.

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-18**  (ID: `11199568`)

Description:
(17) Last X2-U Guard Timer expires

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-18.0-2**  (ID: `11199581`)

Description:
 At last X2-U GT expiry, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall end counting the time of the burst for the report (thpTimeDl) [Before PR794319]due to there is no any other GT running nor any PDCP SDU[CNI-112795]/PDU[End CNI-112795] waiting for transmission[CNI-112795]/retransmission[End CNI-112795] to 5G-L2-Hi DU or eNB[PR794319] as the gNB buffer is empty[End PR794319] (that is considered as end of the burst).

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-19**  (ID: `11199588`)

Description:
(18) Alternative End of Burst

---

**8.2.4.2.2.0-3.0-19.0-1**  (ID: `11199595`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall detect end of burst after:

o last GT expiry on DDDS arrival OR

o last GT expiry on new SDU receive OR

o bearer delete OR

o bearer modification with nrCellIdentity change

 For each case described above 5G-L2-Hi CU shall update

ThpVolDl according to the formula: ThpVolDl = LteThpVolDl + NrThpVolDl,

where: LteThpVolDl = (PDCP SDU n+1) + (PDCP SDU m)

NrThpVolDl = (PDCP SDU n) + (PDCP SDU m-1)

and

ThpTimeDl according to the formula: last GT expiry - Retention Delay timer expiry.

---

#### 8.2.4.2.3 Exceptions

#### 8.2.4.3.2 Description:

**8.2.4.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11199640`)

Description:
(1) PDCP SDU n

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.3.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11199647`)

Description:
5G-L2-Hi CU shall process PDCP SDU n into PDCP PDU n.



---

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-2 Description: (2) Conditions to proceed further with data transfer from 5G-L2-HI-CU to 5G-L2-HI-DU (ID: 11199654)

**8.2.4.3.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11199660`)

Description:
 Either the bearer should be in Active state when the PDCP SDU is received

 OR the bearer shall be transitioned to Active state from Inactive state, if the bearer was in Inactive state when the PDCP SDU was received.

NOTE : In case the bearer is not active OR the bearer will not become active, PDCP SDU is not sent to RLC.

---

**8.2.4.3.2.0-3**  (ID: `11199666`)

Description:
(3) PDCP PDU n

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.3.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11199674`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU n towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start F1-U GT for PDCP PDU n as per formula: PDCP PDU n Volume/avgEstTput n) + avgPduDelvDelay n.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start F1-U Retention Delay timer as per: avgPduDelvDelay n.

  5G-L2-Hi CU shall consider start of a new burst for 5G leg.

where:

* avgEstTput n and avgPduDelvDelay n can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-4 Description: (4) F1-U Retention Delay Timer and Guard Timer for PDCP PDU n start (ID: 11199683)

**8.2.4.3.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11199690`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall not count F1-U Retention Delay Time to ThpTimeDl5G.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start F1-U Retention Delay timer and GT for PDCP PDU n with sending PDCP PDU n towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

---

**8.2.4.3.2.0-5**  (ID: `11199697`)

Description:

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

**8.2.4.3.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11199704`)

 5G-L2-HI CU shall process PDCP SDU n+1 into PDCP PDU n+1.

**8.2.4.3.2.0-6**  (ID: `11199711`)

Description:
(6) PDCP PDU n+1

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> LTE L2

**8.2.4.3.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11199718`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU n+1 towards LTE L2 and start GT n+1.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start X2-U GT for PDCP PDU n+1 as per formula: (PDCP PDU n+1 Volume/avgEstTputX2 n+1) + avgPduDelvDelayX2 n+1.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start X2-U Retention Delay timer as per: avgPduDelvDelay n+1.

5G-L2-Hi CU shall consider start of a new burst for LTE leg.

where:

* avgEstTputX2 n+1 and avgPduDelvDelayX2 n+1 can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-7 Description: (7) X2-U Retention Delay and Guard Timer for PDCP PDU n+1 start (ID: 11199725)

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start X2-U Retention Delay timer and GT for PDCP PDU n+1 with sending PDCP PDU n+1 towards LTE L2.

---

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-9 Description: (9) X2-U Retention Delay Timer expires (ID: 11199750)

**8.2.4.3.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11199757`)

Description:
 At X2-U Retention Delay Timer expiry, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall start counting the time of the burst for the report (thpTimeDlLte) for LTE leg.

---

Description:

Direction: 5G-L2-HI DU -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5815\_replaced([11222283](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx6t4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

**8.2.4.3.2.0-13**  (ID: `11199804`)

Description:
(13) PDCP PDU m-1

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.3.2.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11199810`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU m-1 towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

 5G-L2-HI CU shall consider PDCP PDU m-1 to the same burst as PDCP PDU n due to F1-U GT is running.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall recalculate F1-U GT for PDCP PDU m as per formula: (PDCP PDU m-1 Volume/avgEstTput m-1) + avgPduDelvDelay m-1.

where:

* avgEstTput m-1 and avgPduDelvDelay m-1 can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-14 Description: (14) F1-U Guard Timer recaculation for PDCP PDU m-1 (ID: 11199817)

**8.2.4.3.2.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11199825`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi shall recalculate F1-U GT for PDCP PDU m-1 with sending of PDCP PDU m-1 towards 5G-L2-Hi DU.

---

Description:
(15) PDCP SDU m

Direction: 5GC -> 5G-L2-HI CU

**8.2.4.3.2.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `11199837`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall process PDCP SDU m into PDCP PDU m.

---

**8.2.4.3.2.0-16**  (ID: `11199844`)

Description:
(16) PDCP PDU m

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU -> LTE L2

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.2.4.3.2.0-16.0-1**  (ID: `11199850`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall send PDCP PDU m towards LTE L2.

 5G-L2-HI CU shall consider PDCP PDU m to the same burst as PDCP PDU n+1 due to X2-U GT is running.

 5G-L2-Hi CU shall recalculate X2-U GT for PDCP PDU m as per formula: (PDCP PDU m Volume/avgEstTputX2 m) + avgPduDelvDelayX2 m.

where:

* avgEstTputX2 m and avgPduDelvDelayX2 m can be calculated as per 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-17 Description: (17) X2-U Guard Timer recalculation for PDCP PDU m (ID: 11199857)

**8.2.4.3.2.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11199863`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi shall recalculate X2-U GT for PDCP PDU m with sending of PDCP PDU m towards LTE L2.

---

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-18 Description: (18) F1-U Guard Timer expires (ID: 11199870)

**8.2.4.3.2.0-18.0-1**  (ID: `11199877`)

Description:
 At last F1-U GT expiry, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall end counting the time of the burst for the report (thpTimeDl5G) for 5G leg due to there is no F1-U GT running (that is considered as end of the burst).

---

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-19 Description: (19) X2-U Guard Timer expires (ID: 11199885)

**8.2.4.3.2.0-19.0-1**  (ID: `11199892`)

Description:
 At last X2-U GT expiry, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall end counting the time of the burst for the report (thpTimeDlLte) for LTE leg due to there is no X2-U GT running (that is considered as end of the burst).

---

##### 8.2.4.3.2.0-20 Description: (20) Alternative End of Burst (ID: 11199900)

**8.2.4.3.2.0-20.0-1**  (ID: `11199906`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi CU shall detect end of burst on 5G or LTE leg after:

o F1-U or X2-U GT expiry on DDDS arrival OR

o F1-U or X2-U GT expiry on new PDU send OR

o bearer delete OR

o bearer modification with nrCellIdentity change

 For each case described above 5G-L2-Hi CU shall update for 5G and LTE leg separately:

ThpVolDl5G according to the formula: ThpVolDl5G = (PDCP PDU n) + (PDCP PDU m-1)

ThpVolDlLte according to the formula: ThpVolDlLte = (PDCP PDU n+1) + (PDCP PDU m)

and

ThpTimeDl5G according to the formula: F1-U GT expiry – F1-U Retention Delay timer expiry

ThpTimeDlLte according to the formula: X2-U GT expiry – X2-U Retention Delay timer expiry

---

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall update ThpVolDl by the sum of RLC PDU m-1 + RLC PDU m +…+ RLC PDU n-1 (RLC PDU n shall be excluded due to is the last TB).

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall update ThpTimeDl by the timestamps received in feedback from L2LO according to the formula: timeSecondLastTbScheduled - timeFirstTbScheduling

#### 8.2.4.4.3 Exceptions

## 8.2.5 DL UE throughput and buffer monitoring

### 8.2.5.1 DL UE throughput monitoring (5G-L2-HI CU)

#### 8.2.5.1.1 Call Flow:

##### 8.2.5.1.1.0-1 Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: 13362545: Call Flow: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "5G-L2-HI Downlink Throughput Monitoring Procedure". The diagram depicts interactions between "5G-L2-HI (CU)", "5G-CP", and "Timer". The procedure begins with the setup of a DRB for a ueldCu with DL Throughput Monitoring parameters. This is followed by a loop that iterates through each eligible DRB of the monitored UE. Inside the loop, a HiUserCu_BearerSetupReq is sent with dlUeTputMonitoringParams , and a HiUserCu_BearerSetupResp is received. Subsequently, DL Throughput Monitoring is activated for the UE, initiated by a HiUserCu_ThroughputMonitoringReq with tputMonitorAction=startDl , and confirmed by a HiUserCu_ThroughputMonitoringResp . The system then starts monitoring DL UE throughput aggregated over all PDU sessions. An optional step allows for DL Throughput parameters modification. If this occurs, a HiUserCu_ThroughputMonitoringReq with tputMonitorAction=modifyThreshold is sent, followed by a HiUserCu_ThroughputMonitoringResp . The diagram then shows a condition where DL UE Throughput is detected to be less than thresholdDlUeTput . This triggers the start of rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMsec , and throughput monitoring continues during this timer period. An alternative (alt) scenario is presented for when the timer expires and the throughput is still below the threshold. This leads to the expiry of rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec , confirming a DL Low Throughput event. A HiUserCu_ThroughputMonitoringInd is sent with dlTputStatus=dlLow . Another alternative scenario covers the case where throughput rises to or above the threshold during the timer period. This results in stopping rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec and returning to normal monitoring. Finally, another optional step (opt) is shown for when the throughput recovers after a low indication has been sent. This is detected when DL UE Throughput is greater than or equal to thresholdDlUeTput . A HiUserCu_ThroughputMonitoringInd is sent with dlTputStatus=dlHigh . This triggers the deactivation of DL Throughput Monitoring for the monitored UE, initiated by a HiUserCu_ThroughputMonitoringReq with tputMonitorAction=stopDl , and confirmed by a HiUserCu_ThroughputMonitoringResp . The participants in the diagram are: - 5G-L2-HI (CU) - 5G-CP - Timer[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/f4b690d2-cbec-4779-b343-2025732544ee.png[/image_path][/image-0] (ID: 13362545)

#### 8.2.5.1.2 Description:

**8.2.5.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `13364515`)

Description:
**(1)** HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq\*\*\*\*

Direction: 5G-CP-NRT - > 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: [10987413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WWh6Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13364524`)

Description:
After reception of HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq containing DL throughput monitoring parameters ([dlUeTputMonitoringParams](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-nSPk9T-EfCnq6aYkXj8Pw)) for a specific DRB of the monitored UE, 5G-L2-HI shall:

* store these parameters,
* create the UE context (see [13372373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_hgJbSPqjEfCPDo8cGBoqIw))

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `13364517`)

Description:
**(2)** HiUserCu\_BearerSetupResp\*\*\*\*

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU - > 5G-CP-NRT

Message definition: [10987478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WXI8vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13364525`)

Description:
5G-L2-HI completes the bearer setup and responds with HiUserCu\_BearerModifyResp to confirm the DRB is configured with monitoring parameters.

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-3**  (ID: `13364526`)

Description:
(3) HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringReq

Direction: 5G-CP-NRT - > 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: [13247387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_WESdbMRoEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13364527`)

Description:
Upon reception of HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringReq with tputMonitorAction=startDl, refer to [13372392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2a4IwfqjEfCPDo8cGBoqIw).

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-4**  (ID: `13364531`)

Description:
(4) HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringResp

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU - > 5G-CP-NRT

Message definition: [13247391](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_m2i5scRoEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13364532`)

Description:
5G-L2-HI activates DL throughput measurement aggregated over all PDU sessions for the UE and responds with HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringResp. L2-HI begins continuous monitoring against the configured threshold (thresholdDlUeTput).

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-6**  (ID: `13364586`)

Description:
(6) HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringReq

Direction: 5G-CP-NRT - > 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: [13247387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_WESdbMRoEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `13364587`)

Description:
Upon reception of HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringReq with tputMonitorAction=modifyThreshold, refer to [13372399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9gqfs_qjEfCPDo8cGBoqIw).

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-7**  (ID: `13364588`)

Description:
(7) HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringResp

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU - > 5G-CP-NRT

Message definition: [13247391](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_m2i5scRoEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `13364589`)

Description:
5G-L2-HI applies the modified parameter and responds with HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringResp.

---

##### 8.2.5.1.2.0-8 Description: (8) start rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec timer (ID: 13364604)

**8.2.5.1.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `13364606`)

Description:
Upon detection of low DL threshold event (DL UE throughput has fallen below thresholdDlUeTput), 5G-L2-HI shall start the [rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9UD4QcbIEfCYBIz6acpPHw) timer.

---

##### 8.2.5.1.2.0-9 Description: (9) Alternative for rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec expiry (Low Throughput Detection with Hysteresis) (ID: 13364629)

**8.2.5.1.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `13364630`)

Description:
The [rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9UD4QcbIEfCYBIz6acpPHw) timer expires. 5G-L2-HI verifies that throughput remains below the threshold and confirms a sustained low throughput condition and proceed to step 10.

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-10**  (ID: `13364644`)

Description:
(10) HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringInd

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU - > 5G-CP-NRT

Message definition: [13247406](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_O_vAEsRpEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `13364645`)

Description:
Upon the [rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9UD4QcbIEfCYBIz6acpPHw) timer expiry (step 9), 5G-L2-HI shall send HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringInd with dlTputStatus=dlLow to 5G-CP-NRT to report the confirmed low DL throughput threshold event.

---

##### 8.2.5.1.2.0-11 Description: (11) Alternative for rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec stop (Throughput Recovery During Hysteresis) (ID: 13364642)

**8.2.5.1.2.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `13364643`)

Description:
If UE DL throughput rises to or above the thresholdDlUeTput value during the hysteresis period, 5G-L2-HI shall stop the [rdLowTputHysteresisPeriodMSec](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9UD4QcbIEfCYBIz6acpPHw) timer and returns to normal monitoring state without sending a low throughput indication.

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-13**  (ID: `13364655`)

Description:
(13) HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringInd

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU - > 5G-CP-NRT

Message definition: [13247406](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_O_vAEsRpEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `13364656`)

Description:
After a low throughput indication was sent (step 10), if 5G-L2-HI detects that DL UE throughput has recovered (equal to or above thresholdDlUeTput), refer to [13372405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_sHh0N_qkEfCPDo8cGBoqIw).

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-14**  (ID: `13364661`)

Direction: 5G-CP-NRT - > 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: [13247387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_WESdbMRoEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `13364662`)

Description:
Upon reception of HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringReq with tputMonitorAction=stopDl for the given ueIdCu, refer to [13372402](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_dX0egvqkEfCPDo8cGBoqIw).

Direction: 5G-L2-HI CU - > 5G-CP-NRT

---

**8.2.5.1.2.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `13364664`)

Description:
5G-L2-HI stops all DL throughput measurements and monitoring for the UE, cancels any active hysteresis timer, and responds with HiUserCu\_ThroughputMonitoringResp.

#### 8.2.5.1.3 Exceptions:

## 8.2.6 Dummy load generation in the DL slots

### 8.2.6.1 UE selection for dummy load generation

#### 8.2.6.1.1 UE selection for dummy load generation in P(S)cell

**8.2.6.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11200159`)

UE selection for dummy load generation in P(S)cell
As explained in (5G\_UP\_12118\_replaced([11348370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubUy-PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS selects the UE instance(s) for dummy load generation on its P(S)Cell by comparing the C-RNTI and the P(S)Cell lcrId with the rdDummyLoadDlLcrIdAndRnti (5G\_L2\_12666\_replaced([11189582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[5G-L2-PS] gets the P(S)Cell lcrId from PsCell\_CellSetupReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) lcrId parameter.

Thanks to the [5G-L2-PS] implementation, all requirements apply both to FR1 and FR2.

---

#### 8.2.6.1.2 UE selection for dummy load generation in Scell

**8.2.6.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11200173`)

UE selection for dummy load generation in Scell
As explained in (5G\_UP\_12118\_replaced([11348370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubUy-PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the [5G-L2-PS] P(S)Cell instance selects the UE instance(s) for dummy load generation by comparing the C-RNTI and the P(S)Cell lcrId with the rdDummyLoadDlLcrIdAndRnti (5G\_L2\_12666\_replaced([11189582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The [5G-L2-PS] Scell instance knows that the UE context is configured on the Scell thanks to PsUser\_UserSetupReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_389\_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ueAddCause = SCellAddition.

Per 3GPP: NCI = gNodeB ID \* 2 ^ (36 -gNodeB ID Length) + Sector ID

As such, the lcrId length could 4 to 14 bits depending on gNodeB ID length.

The [5G-L2-PS] Scell instance approximates the gNodeB ID Length with the maximum value of:

* 4 (as defined by the 3GPP)
* The position of the most significant bit of the P(S)Cell lcrId defined in rdDummyLoadDlLcrIdAndRnti (5G\_L2\_12666\_replaced([11189582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The [5G-L2-PS] Scell instance gets the P(S)cell nrCellIdentity from the PsUser\_UserSetupReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_389\_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) CellConfigParam.  
Thanks to the approximation of the gNodeB ID Length, the [5G-L2-PS] Scell instance gets an approximated lcrId of the P(S)cell from the P(S)cell nrCellIdentity.

Thanks to the [5G-L2-PS] implementation, all requirements apply both to FR1 and FR2.

---

### 8.2.6.2 DL MAC-layer dummy load generation

#### 8.2.6.2.1 DL MAC-layer dummy load generation in P(S)cell

**8.2.6.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11200193`)

DL MAC-layer dummy load generation in P(S)cell
On the P(S)Cell, for the selected UE dummy load generation for [CNI-101738], the Core Network shall continuously send DL data otherwise [5G-CU-UP] will trigger a bearer release.

The [L2-HI-RLC] bearer context for this UE will then repetitively receives DL data from [5G-CU-UP] and sends the DL data the [5G-L2-LO] context of the P(S)Cell.

[5G-L2-LO] will send regularly to [5G-L2-PS] LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Upon reception of the LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). for the UE selected for the dummy load generation, the [5G-L2-PS] P(S)Cell instance overwrites the bufferedBytes with the value rdDummyLoadDlBsr (5G\_L2\_12668\_replaced([11189594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The selected UE for the dummy load generation becomes then candidate for DL scheduling.

When the selected UE for dummy load generation is candidate for DL scheduling, [5G-L2-PS] P(S)Cell instance does not decrease the internal overwritten data corresponding to bufferedBytes in LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 8.2.6.2.2 DL MAC-layer dummy load generation in Scell

**8.2.6.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11200208`)

DL MAC-layer dummy load generation in Scell
On the SCell, for the UE selected for dummy load generation with [CNI-101738] the Core Network shall continuously send DL data otherwise [5G-CU-UP] will trigger a bearer release.

The [L2-HI-RLC] bearer context for this UE will then repetitively receive DL data from [5G-CU-UP].

If the DL input data throughput is high enough, [L2-HI-RLC] bearer context for this UE may send the DL data to the [5G-L2-LO] context of the SCell.

In such a case the mechanism explained for the P(S)Cell in (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5268\_replaced([11200193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgL7EfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) applies to the [5G-L2-PS] Scell context.

But most of the time, [5G-L2-LO] of the Scell UE context may never receive any data from [L2-HI-RLC].

Therefore [5G-L2-LO] of the Scell UE context will never send LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to the [5G-L2\_PS] Scell UE context.

[5G-L2\_PS] Scell UE context uses the reception of PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_653\_replaced([10979413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU0Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with parameter ModifType = START when the Scell is activated by P(S)Cell, as a trigger to overwrite the [5G-L2-PS] internal data that is normally updated by the value bufferedBytes in LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Thanks to this overwriting, the UE dummy load generation becomes candidate for DL scheduing as explained for the [5G-L2\_PS] P(S)Cell in (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5268\_replaced([11200193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgL7EfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

### 8.2.6.3 Scell Activation

#### 8.2.6.3.1 Scell Activation in P(S)cell

**8.2.6.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11200230`)

Scell Activation in P(S)cell
As explained in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5268\_replaced([11200193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgL7EfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), on the P(S)Cell, the [5G-L2-LO] will send regularely to [5G-L2-PS] the LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Upon reception of the LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). for the selected UE dummy load generation, the [5G-L2-PS] P(S)Cell instance overwrites the currentDrbBufferSize corresponding to the current DL RLC SDU buffer size with the value rdDummyLoadDlBsr (5G\_L2\_12668\_replaced([11189594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) multiplied by the number of Component Carrier defined for this UE context.

This overwriting forces the [5G-L2-PS] to activate the Scell(s).

---

#### 8.2.6.3.2 Scell Activation in Scell

**8.2.6.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11200246`)

Scell Activation in Scell
Once the Scell is activated as explained in (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5270\_replaced([11200230](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgL7FvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the [5G-L2-PS] Scell starts sending DL data as explained in (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5269\_replaced([11200208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgL7E_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Unfortunately with the current  [5G-L2-PS] implementation, the sending of those DL data padding on the Scell, does not prevent the Scell to be deactivated.

To prevent the  [5G-L2-PS] Scell to be deactivated for the UE dummy load context,  [5G-L2-PS] Scell does not inform [5G-L2-PS] P(S)cell when the [5G-L2-PS] Scell inactivity timer expires.

Depending on the [5G-L2-HI] (RLC) setting, [5G-L2-HI] may forward some data to the Scell [5G-L2-LO] context. In this case, The Scell [5G-L2-LO] context wil send the Scell [5G-L2-PS] context a LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In this case, the Scell Inactivity timer in the Scell [5G-L2-PS] context is not stopped by [CNI-101738] in order to allow the Scell desactivation when the Dummy load is stopped.

---

### 8.2.6.4 Scell addition Buffer based [CB008311]

**8.2.6.4.0-1**  (ID: `11200261`)

Scell addition Buffer based [CB008311]
As explained in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5268\_replaced([11200193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgL7EfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), on the P(S)Cell, the [5G-L2-LO] will send regularly to [5G-L2-PS] the LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Upon reception of the LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_869\_replaced([10984606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBKwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). for the selected UE dummy load generation, the [5G-L2-PS] overwrites the currentDrbBufferSize corresponding current DL RLC SDU buffer size with the value rdDummyLoadDlBsr (5G\_L2\_12668\_replaced([11189594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) multiplied by the number of Component Carrier defined for this UE context.

When the feature [CB008311] is activated, this overwriting forces the [5G-L2-PS] P(S)Cell instance to send to [5G-CP-RT] the PsUser\_BufferCriterionInd message (5G\_L2\_IF\_4557\_replaced([10978239](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VSK4_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as defined in [CB008311]. This overflow message will ultimately lead to a Scell addition.

---

### 8.2.6.5 Scell Activation and Addition in external Scell for inter DU CA

#### 8.2.6.5.0-1 Scell Activation and Addition in external Scell for inter DU CA In case of inter DU Carrier Aggregation, the Rad parameters of the CNI-101738 need to be also polulated in the remote DU. As explained in (5G_L1L2_FLOW_5269_replaced( 11200208 )) the Scell dummy load generation is triggered in [5G-L2-PS] Scell by the reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq (5G_L2_IF_653_replaced( 10979413 )). The message PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq (5G_L2_IF_653_replaced( 10979413 )) is sent once at Scell Activation time. As such it is important to set the Rad Parameters first in the Remote DU running the Scell before setting the  Rad Parameters in local DU running the Pcell. (ID: 11200275)

### 8.2.6.6 Rad Parameter setting for the dummy load

#### 8.2.6.6.1 Rad Parameter setting for the dummy load on P(S)Cell

##### 8.2.6.6.1.0-1 Rad Parameter setting for the dummy load on P(S)Cell For the P(S)cell dummy load generation, the Rad Parameters rdEnableDummyLoadDl (5G_L2_12664_replaced( 11189570 )), rdDummyLoadDlLcrIdAndRnti (5G_L2_12666_replaced( 11189582 )) and rdDummyLoadDlBsr (5G_L2_12668_replaced( 11189594 )) can be set in any order. As explained in (5G_L1L2_FLOW_5268_replaced( 11200193 )) the P(S)Cell dummy load generation is triggered in [5G-L2-PS] P(S)Cell by the reception of LoCtrl_DlBufferStatusInd (5G_L2_IF_869_replaced( 10984606 )). The message LoCtrl_DlBufferStatusInd (5G_L2_IF_869_replaced( 10984606 )) is sent repetitively by [5G-L2-LO]. As such or order of setting of the Rad Parameters is irrelevant. (ID: 11200297)

#### 8.2.6.6.2 Rad Parameter setting for the dummy load on the Scell or external Scell

**8.2.6.6.2.0-1**  (ID: `11200312`)

Rad Parameter setting for the dummy load on the Scell or external Scell
For the Scell dummy load generation, the Rad Parameters rdDummyLoadDlLcrIdAndRnti (5G\_L2\_12666\_replaced([11189582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdDummyLoadDlBsr (5G\_L2\_12668\_replaced([11189594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) must be set first and the Rad Parametersr dEnableDummyLoadDl (5G\_L2\_12664\_replaced([11189570](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) must be set in a separated second step.

As explained in (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5269\_replaced([11200208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgL7E_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) the Scell dummy load generation is triggered in [5G-L2-PS] Scell by the reception of PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_653\_replaced([10979413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU0Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The message PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_653\_replaced([10979413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU0Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is sent once at Scell Activation time. As such it is important to set the Rad Parameters in the right order.

To change the UE target for dummy load, the Rad Parametersr dEnableDummyLoadDl (5G\_L2\_12664\_replaced([11189570](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) must be set to disable (0) first. Then the Rad Parameters rdDummyLoadDlLcrIdAndRnti (5G\_L2\_12666\_replaced([11189582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdDummyLoadDlBsr (5G\_L2\_12668\_replaced([11189594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) can be set with a new value. The dummy load generation needs to be re activated in a thirst step by setting Rad Parametersr dEnableDummyLoadDl (5G\_L2\_12664\_replaced([11189570](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to enable (1).

---

The diagram shows a "Loop" that iterates through available "[5GC002093-A]" within a "DLsubcell". Inside this loop, a message "DIdat\_PatternConfigReq" is sent from "5G-L2-PS" to "5G-L1-DL".

Beamforming Pattern ID with eCPRI
5G-L1-DL
5G-L2-PS
Loop For each [5GC002093-A] available [End 5GC002093-A]
DLsubcell
DIdat\_PatternConfigReq[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3276.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
File "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_573\_Beamforming Pattern ID with eCPRI.signalling" stored at:
 
With eCPRI fronthaul, pattern IDs are provided by 5G-L2-PS for all types of slots: data, broadcast (PSS, SSS, PBCH) and PRACH. A different format is used for PRACH. Messages are sent to 5G-L1-DL instance for each [5GC002093-A] available [End 5GC002093-A] DL subcell.
 
Notes:
\* 5G-L1-DL may ignore the messages, as in eCPRI the beamforming control is based on regular send requests
\* [5GC002093-A] "Available subcell" refers to subcell pooling, see 5G\_UP\_1751\_replaced([11372528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud93QfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End 5GC002093-A]
\* [5GC000399-KX] In all eCPRI configurations (FR1/FR2, BF/nonBF), 5G-L1-DL generates the fast control plane packet, based on channel-specific send/receive request messages. 5G-L2-PS does not send patternConfigReq messages.  [End 5GC000399-KX]

**Title:** Concurrent Handover or Bearer Type Change Procedure
**Components/Lifelines:**
\* **Target-gNB:** This lifeline has a box labeled "Target-gNB" at the top, with a sub-box labeled "5G-L2-HI (CU)". This component appears twice, once at the top and once at the bottom.
\* **Timer:** This lifeline has a box labeled "Timer" at the top and another at the bottom.
**Diagram Elements:**
\* **Yellow Note:** A yellow rectangular note is positioned above the "Target-gNB" lifeline. It contains the text: "DL Data Forwarding is ongoing AND EndMarker has not been received by Target-gNB OR End Marker Timer is running".
\* **Alt Fragment:** An "alt" fragment encloses several "ref" fragments, indicating alternative execution paths.
\* **Ref Fragments:** Six "ref" fragments are nested within the "alt" fragment. Each "ref" fragment represents a specific procedure or event and is labeled with a number and a description:
1. **(1) SA Inter-gNB Mobility (11193024)**
2. **(2) SA Intra-gNB Mobility (12783633)**
3. **(3) NSA Inter-gNB Mobility (11188971)**
4. **(4) NSA Intra-gNB Mobility (13336986)**
5. **(5) NR-DC Inter-gNB PSCell Addition (11190335)**
6. **(6) NR-DC Intra-gNB PSCell Addition (11189529)**
\* **Message/Action:** Below the "ref" fragments, there is a dashed line extending from the "Target-gNB" lifeline to the "Timer" lifeline, with the label "(7) terminate endMarkerTimer". An "X" symbol is placed at the end of this dashed line, indicating termination or cancellation.

---

**8.2.8.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `13429969`)

Concurrent Handover or Bearer Type Change Procedure
When 5G-L2-HI (CU) in target gNB receives HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause = Suspend (step 2 or 4) or cause = BearerRelease (step 1 or 3 or 5) or cause = AddSecondaryLink (step 6), while DL data forwarding is ongoing, AND the DL End Marker has not been received or the endMarkerTimer is still running, then 5G-L2-HI (CU) in gNB-MN shall perform the Concurrent Handover Procedures as defined in [13465873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3z_5QDS2EfGxldjOZQLezQ).
